Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n     4→\n     5→## Step Graph Design\n     6→\n     7→### Step Definition Pattern\n     8→\n     9→Every workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n    10→\n    11→```python\n    12→Step(\n    13→    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    14→    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    15→    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    16→    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    17→    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    18→    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    19→    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    20→    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    21→    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n    22→)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→### Gate Mode Selection\n    26→\n    27→Choose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n    28→- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n    29→- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n    30→\n    31→Rule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n    32→- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n    33→- Milestone scope → configurable\n    34→- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n    35→\n    36→### Parallel Group Pattern\n    37→\n    38→Steps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n    39→\n    40→```python\n    41→steps = [\n    42→    single_step_1,\n    43→    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    44→    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n    45→]\n    46→```\n    47→\n    48→The generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n    49→\n    50→### Dependency Rules\n    51→\n    52→- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n    53→- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n    54→- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n    55→- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n    56→\n    57→## Model Design Patterns\n    58→\n    59→### Config Model\n    60→\n    61→Always extend `PipelineConfig`:\n    62→\n    63→```python\n    64→@dataclass\n    65→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    66→    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    67→    # Required: identify the input\n    68→    source_path: Path\n    69→\n    70→    # Optional: control behavior\n    71→    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n    72→\n    73→    # Computed paths\n    74→    @property\n    75→    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n    76→        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n    77→\n    78→    @property\n    79→    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n    80→        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n    81→```\n    82→\n    83→### Status Enum\n    84→\n    85→Sprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n    86→\n    87→```python\n    88→class StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    89→    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    90→    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    91→    PASS = \"pass\"\n    92→    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    93→    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    94→    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    95→    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    96→    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    97→    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    98→    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n    99→```\n   100→\n   101→### Result Model\n   102→\n   103→Extend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n   104→\n   105→```python\n   106→@dataclass\n   107→class MyStepResult(StepResult):\n   108→    exit_code: int | None = None\n   109→    started_at: float | None = None\n   110→    finished_at: float | None = None\n   111→    output_bytes: int = 0\n   112→    error_bytes: int = 0\n   113→    # Domain-specific signals:\n   132→    last_step_id: str | None = None\n   133→    current_artifact: str | None = None\n   134→    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n   135→```\n   136→\n   137→## Gate Design Patterns\n   138→\n   139→### Gate Criteria Tiers\n   140→\n   141→```python\n   142→# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\n   143→EXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"exempt\")\n   144→\n   145→# Light: file exists and non-empty\n   146→LIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"light\")\n   147→\n   148→# Standard: structural validation\n   149→STANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n   150→    tier=\"standard\",\n   151→    min_lines=50,\n   152→    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n   153→)\n   154→\n   155→# Strict: structural + semantic validation\n   156→STRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n   157→    tier=\"strict\",\n   158→    min_lines=100,\n   159→    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n   160→    semantic_checks=[\n   161→        SemanticCheck(name=\"no_heading_gaps\", fn=_no_heading_gaps),\n   162→        SemanticCheck(name=\"refs_resolve\", fn=_cross_refs_resolve),\n   163→    ],\n   164→)\n   165→```\n   166→\n   167→### Semantic Check Functions\n   168→\n   169→Semantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n   170→\n   171→```python\n   172→def _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   173→    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n   174→    # ... implementation ...\n   175→    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n   176→\n   177→def _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   178→    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n   179→    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n   180→    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n   181→    missing = required - present\n   182→    if missing:\n   183→        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n   184→    return (True, \"\")\n   185→```\n   186→\n   187→### Frontmatter Validation\n   188→\n   189→The shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n   190→\n   191→```yaml\n   192→---\n   193→title: Diff Analysis\n   194→status: complete\n   195→diff_points: 12\n   196→convergence_ready: true\n   197→---\n   198→```\n   199→\n   200→## Prompt Design Patterns\n   201→\n   202→### Prompt Builder Structure\n   203→\n   204→Each step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n   205→\n   206→```python\n   207→def build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n   208→    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n   209→\n   210→Source: {source_path}\n   211→Depth: {config.depth}\n   212→\n   213→## Required Output Format\n   214→\n   215→Write your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n   216→\n   217→```yaml\n   218→---\n   219→title: Analysis Report\n   220→status: complete\n   221→finding_count: <integer>\n   222→---\n   223→```\n   224→\n   225→## Sections Required\n   226→\n   227→### Summary\n   228→Brief overview of findings.\n   229→\n   230→### Findings\n   231→Numbered list of findings with evidence.\n   232→\n   233→### Recommendations\n   234→Actionable next steps.\n   235→\n   236→## Machine-Readable Markers\n   237→\n   238→At the end of your output, include:\n   239→```\n   240→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n   241→```\n   242→or\n   243→```\n   244→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n   245→```\n   246→\"\"\"\n   247→```\n   248→\n   249→### Key Prompt Rules\n   250→\n   251→1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n   252→2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n   253→3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n   254→4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n   255→5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n   256→\n   257→### Input Embedding Pattern\n   258→\n   259→```python\n   260→def _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n   261→    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n   262→    file_args = []\n   263→    for input_path in inputs:\n   264→        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n   265→        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n   266→            content = full_path.read_text()\n   267→            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n   268→        else:\n   269→            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n   270→    return prompt, file_args\n   271→```\n   272→\n   273→## Executor Design Patterns\n   274→\n   275→### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n   276→\n   277→The sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n   278→\n   279→```python\n   280→def execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n   281→    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n   282→    verify_claude_binary()\n   283→\n   284→    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n   285→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   286→    logger = MyLogger(config)\n   287→    tui = MyTUI(config)\n   288→    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n   289→    result = MyResult(config=config)\n   290→    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n   291→\n   292→    # 3. Start TUI\n   293→    tui.start()\n   294→\n   295→    try:\n   296→        for step in config.steps:\n   297→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   298→                break\n   299→\n   300→            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n   301→            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n   302→            monitor.start()\n   303→\n   304→            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n   305→            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n   306→            process.start()\n   307→\n   308→            # 6. Supervision loop\n   309→            while process.is_running():\n   310→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   311→                    process.stop()\n   312→                    break\n   313→\n   314→                state = monitor.get_state()\n   315→\n   316→                # Stall detection\n   317→                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n   318→                    process.stop()\n   319→                    break\n   320→\n   321→                # TUI update\n   322→                tui.update(step, state)\n   323→                time.sleep(0.5)\n   324→\n   325→            # 7. Classify result\n   326→            monitor.stop()\n   327→            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n   328→\n   329→            # 8. Record and decide\n   330→            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n   331→            result.add(step_result)\n   332→            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n   333→\n   334→            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   335→                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n   336→                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n   337→                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n   338→                result.outcome = HALTED\n   339→                break\n   340→\n   341→    finally:\n   342→        tui.stop()\n   343→        monitor.stop()\n   344→        signal_handler.restore()\n   345→\n   346→    return result\n   347→```\n   348→\n   349→### Status Classification\n   350→\n   351→Map every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n   352→\n   353→```python\n   354→def determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n   355→    # 1. Hard failures\n   356→    if exit_code == 124:\n   357→        return TIMEOUT\n   358→    if exit_code != 0:\n   359→        return ERROR\n   360→\n   361→    # 2. Check for structured result file\n   362→    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n   363→    if result_path.exists():\n   364→        content = result_path.read_text()\n   365→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n   366→            return HALT\n   367→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n   368→            return PASS\n   369→        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n   370→\n   371→    # 3. Check for output without result\n   372→    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n   373→    if output_path.exists():\n   374→        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n   375→            return INCOMPLETE\n   376→        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n   377→\n   378→    # 4. No output at all\n   379→    return ERROR\n   380→```\n   381→\n   382→## Integration Patterns\n   383→\n   384→### main.py Registration\n   385→\n   386→```python\n   387→# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\n   388→from superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\n   389→app.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n   390→```\n   391→\n   392→### Click Command Group\n   393→\n   394→```python\n   395→@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\n   396→def my_pipeline_group():\n   397→    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n   398→    pass\n   399→\n   400→@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n   401→@click.argument(\"source\")\n   402→@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n   403→@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n   404→@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n   405→@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n   406→@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\n   407→def run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n   408→    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n   409→    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n   410→    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n   411→    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n   412→```\n   413→\n   414→## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n   415→\n   416→For pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n   417→\n   418→```python\n   419→from superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n   420→\n   421→@dataclass\n   422→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n   423→    max_turns: int = 200\n   424→    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n   425→    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n   426→\n   427→# In executor:\n   428→ledger = TurnLedger(\n   429→    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n   430→    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n   431→    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n   432→)\n   433→\n   434→# Before launching a step:\n   435→if not ledger.can_launch():\n   436→    result.outcome = HALTED\n   437→    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n   438→    break\n   439→\n   440→# After step completes, count actual turns used:\n   441→actual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\n   442→ledger.debit(actual_turns)\n   443→\n   444→# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\n   445→if actual_turns < allocated:\n   446→    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n   447→```\n   448→\n   449→## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n   450→\n   451→For pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n   452→\n   453→```python\n   454→def setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n   455→    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n   456→    env = os.environ.copy()\n   457→\n   458→    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n   459→    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n   460→\n   461→    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n   462→    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n   463→\n   464→    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n   465→    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n   466→    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n   467→    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n   468→\n   469→    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n   470→    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n   471→    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n   472→    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n   473→\n   474→    return env\n   475→```\n   476→\n   477→## Context Injection Pattern\n   478→\n   479→Prior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n   480→\n   481→```python\n   482→def build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n   483→    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n   484→    base_prompt = step.prompt\n   485→\n   486→    if not prior_results:\n   487→        return base_prompt\n   488→\n   489→    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n   490→    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n   491→        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n   492→        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n   493→\n   494→    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n   495→```\n   496→\n   497→## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n   498→\n   499→On halt, generate actionable resume information:\n   500→\n   501→```python\n   502→@dataclass\n   503→class MyResult:\n   504→    # ... other fields ...\n   505→\n   506→    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n   507→        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n   508→        if not self.halt_step:\n   509→            return None\n   510→        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n   511→                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n   512→        return (\n   513→            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n   514→            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n   515→            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n   516→        )\n   517→\n   518→    @property\n   519→    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n   520→        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n   521→        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n   522→                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n   523→        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n   524→```\n   525→\n   526→## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n   527→\n   528→Not all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n   529→\n   530→```python\n   531→def execute_step(step, config):\n   532→    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n   533→    if step.prompt == \"\":\n   534→        # Pure programmatic — run directly\n   535→        return run_programmatic_step(step, config)\n   536→    else:\n   537→        # Claude-assisted — launch subprocess\n   538→        return run_claude_step(step, config)\n   539→\n   540→def run_programmatic_step(step, config) -> StepResult:\n   541→    \"\"\"Execute a pure-programmatic step without Claude.\"\"\"\n   542→    started = time.time()\n   543→    try:\n   544→        # Call the step's implementation function\n   545→        PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS[step.id](config)\n   546→        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.PASS,\n   547→                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n   548→    except Exception as e:\n   549→        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n   550→                         gate_failure_reason=str(e),\n   551→                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n   552→```\n   553→\n   554→## Gate Display State Machine (for TUI)\n   555→\n   556→Model gate states as explicit transitions for richer UX:\n   557→\n   558→```python\n   559→class GateDisplayState(Enum):\n   560→    NONE = \"none\"\n   561→    CHECKING = \"checking\"\n   562→    PASS = \"pass\"\n   563→    FAIL_DEFERRED = \"fail_deferred\"\n   564→    REMEDIATING = \"remediating\"\n   565→    REMEDIATED = \"remediated\"\n   566→    HALT = \"halt\"\n   567→\n   568→    @property\n   569→    def icon(self) -> str:\n   570→        return {\n   571→            \"none\": \" \", \"checking\": \"...\",\n   572→            \"pass\": \"ok\", \"fail_deferred\": \"!\",\n   573→            \"remediating\": \"~\", \"remediated\": \"ok\",\n   574→            \"halt\": \"X\",\n   575→        }[self.value]\n   576→```\n   577→"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01ARrV4zNqqgtQKuPjmHQfkE","session_id":"6d48e8db-6652-4750-84bd-06ac42d65350","uuid":"4fe36b08-c17d-4450-987b-f35924b7c81c"}

This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n     4→\n     5→## Step Graph Design\n     6→\n     7→### Step Definition Pattern\n     8→\n     9→Every workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n    10→\n    11→```python\n    12→Step(\n    13→    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    14→    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    15→    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    16→    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    17→    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    18→    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    19→    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    20→    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    21→    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n    22→)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→### Gate Mode Selection\n    26→\n    27→Choose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n    28→- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n    29→- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n    30→\n    31→Rule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n    32→- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n    33→- Milestone scope → configurable\n    34→- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n    35→\n    36→### Parallel Group Pattern\n    37→\n    38→Steps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n    39→\n    40→```python\n    41→steps = [\n    42→    single_step_1,\n    43→    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    44→    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n    45→]\n    46→```\n    47→\n    48→The generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n    49→\n    50→### Dependency Rules\n    51→\n    52→- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n    53→- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n    54→- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n    55→- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n    56→\n    57→## Model Design Patterns\n    58→\n    59→### Config Model\n    60→\n    61→Always extend `PipelineConfig`:\n    62→\n    63→```python\n    64→@dataclass\n    65→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    66→    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    67→    # Required: identify the input\n    68→    source_path: Path\n    69→\n    70→    # Optional: control behavior\n    71→    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n    72→\n    73→    # Computed paths\n    74→    @property\n    75→    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n    76→        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n    77→\n    78→    @property\n    79→    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n    80→        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n    81→```\n    82→\n    83→### Status Enum\n    84→\n    85→Sprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n    86→\n    87→```python\n    88→class StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    89→    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    90→    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    91→    PASS = \"pass\"\n    92→    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    93→    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    94→    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    95→    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    96→    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    97→    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    98→    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n    99→```\n   100→\n   101→### Result Model\n   102→\n   103→Extend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n   104→\n   105→```python\n   106→@dataclass\n   107→class MyStepResult(StepResult):\n   108→    exit_code: int | None = None\n   109→    started_at: float | None = None\n   110→    finished_at: float | None = None\n   111→    output_bytes: int = 0\n   112→    error_bytes: int = 0\n   113→    # Domain-specific fields:\n   114→    artifacts_produced: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n   115→    gate_details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n   116→```\n   117→\n   118→### Monitor State\n   119→\n   120→Domain-specific signals extracted from NDJSON output:\n   121→\n   122→```python\n   123→@dataclass\n   124→class MyMonitorState:\n   125→    output_bytes: int = 0\n   126→    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n   127→    events_received: int = 0\n   128→    lines_total: int = 0\n   129→    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n   130→    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n   131→    # Domain-specific signals:\n   132→    last_step_id: str | None = None\n   133→    current_artifact: str | None = None\n   134→    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n   135→```\n   136→\n   137→## Gate Design Patterns\n   138→\n   139→### Gate Criteria Tiers\n   140→\n   141→```python\n   142→# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\n   143→EXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"exempt\")\n   144→\n   145→# Light: file exists and non-empty\n   146→LIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"light\")\n   147→\n   148→# Standard: structural validation\n   149→STANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n   150→    tier=\"standard\",\n   151→    min_lines=50,\n   152→    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n   153→)\n   154→\n   155→# Strict: structural + semantic validation\n   156→STRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n   157→    tier=\"strict\",\n   158→    min_lines=100,\n   159→    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n   160→    semantic_checks=[\n   161→        SemanticCheck(name=\"no_heading_gaps\", fn=_no_heading_gaps),\n   162→        SemanticCheck(name=\"refs_resolve\", fn=_cross_refs_resolve),\n   163→    ],\n   164→)\n   165→```\n   166→\n   167→### Semantic Check Functions\n   168→\n   169→Semantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n   170→\n   171→```python\n   172→def _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   173→    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n   174→    # ... implementation ...\n   175→    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n   176→\n   177→def _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   178→    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n   179→    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n   180→    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n   181→    missing = required - present\n   182→    if missing:\n   183→        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n   184→    return (True, \"\")\n   185→```\n   186→\n   187→### Frontmatter Validation\n   188→\n   189→The shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n   190→\n   191→```yaml\n   192→---\n   193→title: Diff Analysis\n   194→status: complete\n   195→diff_points: 12\n   196→convergence_ready: true\n   197→---\n   198→```\n   199→\n   200→## Prompt Design Patterns\n   201→\n   202→### Prompt Builder Structure\n   203→\n   204→Each step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n   205→\n   206→```python\n   207→def build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n   208→    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n   209→\n   210→Source: {source_path}\n   211→Depth: {config.depth}\n   212→\n   213→## Required Output Format\n   214→\n   215→Write your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n   216→\n   217→```yaml\n   218→---\n   219→title: Analysis Report\n   220→status: complete\n   221→finding_count: <integer>\n   222→---\n   223→```\n   224→\n   225→## Sections Required\n   226→\n   227→### Summary\n   228→Brief overview of findings.\n   229→\n   230→### Findings\n   231→Numbered list of findings with evidence.\n   232→\n   233→### Recommendations\n   234→Actionable next steps.\n   235→\n   236→## Machine-Readable Markers\n   237→\n   238→At the end of your output, include:\n   239→```\n   240→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n   241→```\n   242→or\n   243→```\n   244→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n   245→```\n   246→\"\"\"\n   247→```\n   248→\n   249→### Key Prompt Rules\n   250→\n   251→1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n   252→2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n   253→3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n   254→4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n   255→5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n   256→\n   257→### Input Embedding Pattern\n   258→\n   259→```python\n   260→def _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n   261→    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n   262→    file_args = []\n   263→    for input_path in inputs:\n   264→        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n   265→        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n   266→            content = full_path.read_text()\n   267→            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n   268→        else:\n   269→            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n   270→    return prompt, file_args\n   271→```\n   272→\n   273→## Executor Design Patterns\n   274→\n   275→### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n   276→\n   277→The sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n   278→\n   279→```python\n   280→def execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n   281→    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n   282→    verify_claude_binary()\n   283→\n   284→    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n   285→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   286→    logger = MyLogger(config)\n   287→    tui = MyTUI(config)\n   288→    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n   289→    result = MyResult(config=config)\n   290→    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n   291→\n   292→    # 3. Start TUI\n   293→    tui.start()\n   294→\n   295→    try:\n   296→        for step in config.steps:\n   297→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   298→                break\n   299→\n   300→            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n   301→            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n   302→            monitor.start()\n   303→\n   304→            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n   305→            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n   306→            process.start()\n   307→\n   308→            # 6. Supervision loop\n   309→            while process.is_running():\n   310→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   311→                    process.stop()\n   312→                    break\n   313→\n   314→                state = monitor.get_state()\n   315→\n   316→                # Stall detection\n   317→                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n   318→                    process.stop()\n   319→                    break\n   320→\n   321→                # TUI update\n   322→                tui.update(step, state)\n   323→                time.sleep(0.5)\n   324→\n   325→            # 7. Classify result\n   326→            monitor.stop()\n   327→            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n   328→\n   329→            # 8. Record and decide\n   330→            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n   331→            result.add(step_result)\n   332→            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n   333→\n   334→            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   335→                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n   336→                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n   337→                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n   338→                result.outcome = HALTED\n   339→                break\n   340→\n   341→    finally:\n   342→        tui.stop()\n   343→        monitor.stop()\n   344→        signal_handler.restore()\n   345→\n   346→    return result\n   347→```\n   348→\n   349→### Status Classification\n   350→\n   351→Map every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n   352→\n   353→```python\n   354→def determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n   355→    # 1. Hard failures\n   356→    if exit_code == 124:\n   357→        return TIMEOUT\n   358→    if exit_code != 0:\n   359→        return ERROR\n   360→\n   361→    # 2. Check for structured result file\n   362→    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n   363→    if result_path.exists():\n   364→        content = result_path.read_text()\n   365→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n   366→            return HALT\n   367→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n   368→            return PASS\n   369→        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n   370→\n   371→    # 3. Check for output without result\n   372→    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n   373→    if output_path.exists():\n   374→        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n   375→            return INCOMPLETE\n   376→        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n   377→\n   378→    # 4. No output at all\n   379→    return ERROR\n   380→```\n   381→\n   382→## Integration Patterns\n   383→\n   384→### main.py Registration\n   385→\n   386→```python\n   387→# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\n   388→from superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\n   389→app.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n   390→```\n   391→\n   392→### Click Command Group\n   393→\n   394→```python\n   395→@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\n   396→def my_pipeline_group():\n   397→    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n   398→    pass\n   399→\n   400→@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n   401→@click.argument(\"source\")\n   402→@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n   403→@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n   404→@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n   405→@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n   406→@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\n   407→def run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n   408→    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n   409→    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n   410→    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n   411→    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n   412→```\n   413→\n   414→## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n   415→\n   416→For pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n   417→\n   418→```python\n   419→from superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n   420→\n   421→@dataclass\n   422→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n   423→    max_turns: int = 200\n   424→    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n   425→    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n   426→\n   427→# In executor:\n   428→ledger = TurnLedger(\n   429→    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n   430→    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n   431→    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n   432→)\n   433→\n   434→# Before launching a step:\n   435→if not ledger.can_launch():\n   436→    result.outcome = HALTED\n   437→    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n   438→    break\n   439→\n   440→# After step completes, count actual turns used:\n   441→actual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\n   442→ledger.debit(actual_turns)\n   443→\n   444→# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\n   445→if actual_turns < allocated:\n   446→    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n   447→```\n   448→\n   449→## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n   450→\n   451→For pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n   452→\n   453→```python\n   454→def setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n   455→    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n   456→    env = os.environ.copy()\n   457→\n   458→    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n   459→    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n   460→\n   461→    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n   462→    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n   463→\n   464→    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n   465→    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n   466→    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n   467→    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n   468→\n   469→    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n   470→    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n   471→    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n   472→    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n   473→\n   474→    return env\n   475→```\n   476→\n   477→## Context Injection Pattern\n   478→\n   479→Prior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n   480→\n   481→```python\n   482→def build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n   483→    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n   484→    base_prompt = step.prompt\n   485→\n   486→    if not prior_results:\n   487→        return base_prompt\n   488→\n   489→    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n   490→    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n   491→        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n   492→        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n   493→\n   494→    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n   495→```\n   496→\n   497→## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n   498→\n   499→On halt, generate actionable resume information:\n   500→\n   501→```python\n   502→@dataclass\n   503→class MyResult:\n   504→    # ... other fields ...\n   505→\n   506→    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n   507→        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n   508→        if not self.halt_step:\n   509→            return None\n   510→        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n   511→                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n   512→        return (\n   513→            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n   514→            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n   515→            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n   516→        )\n   517→\n   518→    @property\n   519→    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n   520→        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n   521→        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n   522→                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n   523→        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n   524→```\n   525→\n   526→## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n   527→\n   528→Not all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n   529→\n   530→```python\n   531→def execute_step(step, config):\n   532→    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n   533→    if step.prompt == \"\":\n   534→        # Pure programmatic — run directly\n   535→        return run_programmatic_step(step, config)\n   536→    else:\n   537→        # Claude-assisted — launch subprocess\n   538→        return run_claude_step(step, config)\n   539→\n   540→def run_programmatic_step(step, config) -> StepResult:\n   541→    \"\"\"Execute a pure-programmatic step without Claude.\"\"\"\n   542→    started = time.time()\n   543→    try:\n   544→        # This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n     4→\n     5→## Step Graph Design\n     6→\n     7→### Step Definition Pattern\n     8→\n     9→Every workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n    10→\n    11→```python\n    12→Step(\n    13→    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    14→    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    15→    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    16→    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    17→    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    18→    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    19→    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    20→    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n    21→)\n    22→```\n    23→\n    24→### Parallel Group Pattern\n    25→\n    26→Steps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n    27→\n    28→```python\n    29→steps = [\n    30→    single_step_1,\n    31→    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    32→    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n    33→]\n    34→```\n    35→\n    36→The generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n    37→\n    38→### Dependency Rules\n    39→\n    40→- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n    41→- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n    42→- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n    43→- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n    44→\n    45→## Model Design Patterns\n    46→\n    47→### Config Model\n    48→\n    49→Always extend `PipelineConfig`:\n    50→\n    51→```python\n    52→@dataclass\n    53→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    54→    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    55→    # Step recommends stopping\n    84→    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    85→    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    86→    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # ... implementation ...\n   163→    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n   164→\n   165→def _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   166→    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n   167→    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n   168→    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n   169→    missing = required - present\n   170→    if missing:\n   171→        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n   172→    return (True, \"\")\n   173→```\n   174→\n   175→### Frontmatter Validation\n   176→\n   177→The shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n   178→\n   179→```yaml\n   180→---\n   181→title: Diff Analysis\n   182→status: complete\n   183→diff_points: 12\n   184→convergence_ready: true\n   185→---\n   186→```\n   187→\n   188→## Prompt Design Patterns\n   189→\n   190→### Prompt Builder Structure\n   191→\n   192→Each step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n   193→\n   194→```python\n   195→def build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n   196→    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n   197→\n   198→Source: {source_path}\n   199→Depth: {config.depth}\n   200→\n   201→## Required Output Format\n   202→\n   203→Write your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n   204→\n   205→```yaml\n   206→---\n   207→title: Analysis Report\n   208→status: complete\n   209→finding_count: <integer>\n   210→---\n   211→```\n   212→\n   213→## Sections Required\n   214→\n   215→### Summary\n   216→Brief overview of findings.\n   217→\n   218→### Findings\n   219→Numbered list of findings with evidence.\n   220→\n   221→### Recommendations\n   222→Actionable next steps.\n   223→\n   224→## Machine-Readable Markers\n   225→\n   226→At the end of your output, include:\n   227→```\n   228→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n   229→```\n   230→or\n   231→```\n   232→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n   233→```\n   234→\"\"\"\n   235→```\n   236→\n   237→### Key Prompt Rules\n   238→\n   239→1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n   240→2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n   241→3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n   242→4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n   243→5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n   244→\n   245→### Input Embedding Pattern\n   246→\n   247→```python\n   248→def _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n   249→    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n   250→    file_args = []\n   251→    for input_path in inputs:\n   252→        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n   253→        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n   254→            content = full_path.read_text()\n   255→            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n   256→        else:\n   257→            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n   258→    return prompt, file_args\n   259→```\n   260→\n   261→## Executor Design Patterns\n   262→\n   263→### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n   264→\n   265→The sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring:\n   266→\n   267→```python\n   268→async def execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n   269→    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n   270→    verify_claude_binary()\n   271→\n   272→    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n   273→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   274→    logger = MyLogger(config)\n   275→    tui = MyTUI(config)\n   276→    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n   277→    result = MyResult(config=config)\n   278→\n   279→    # 3. Start TUI\n   280→    tui.start()\n   281→\n   282→    try:\n   283→        for step in config.steps:\n   284→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   285→                break\n   286→\n   287→            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n   288→            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n   289→            monitor.start()\n   290→\n   291→            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n   292→            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n   293→            process.start()\n   294→\n   295→            # 6. Supervision loop\n   296→            while process.is_running():\n   297→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   298→                    process.stop()\n   299→                    break\n   300→\n   301→                state = monitor.get_state()\n   302→\n   303→                # Stall detection\n   304→                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n   305→                    process.stop()\n   306→                    break\n   307→\n   308→                # TUI update\n   309→                tui.update(step, state)\n   310→                time.sleep(0.5)\n   311→\n   312→            # 7. Classify result\n   313→            monitor.stop()\n   314→            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n   315→\n   316→            # 8. Record and decide\n   317→            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n   318→            result.add(step_result)\n   319→            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n   320→\n   321→            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   322→                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n   323→                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n   324→                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n   325→                result.outcome = HALTED\n   326→                break\n   327→\n   328→    finally:\n   329→        tui.stop()\n   330→        monitor.stop()\n   331→        signal_handler.restore()\n   332→\n   333→    return result\n   334→```\n   335→\n   336→### Status Classification\n   337→\n   338→Map every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n   339→\n   340→```python\n   341→def determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n   342→    # 1. Hard failures\n   343→    if exit_code == 124:\n   344→        return TIMEOUT\n   345→    if exit_code != 0:\n   346→        return ERROR\n   347→\n   348→    # 2. Check for structured result file\n   349→    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n   350→    if result_path.exists():\n   351→        content = result_path.read_text()\n   352→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n   353→            return HALT\n   354→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n   355→            return PASS\n   356→        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n   357→\n   358→    # 3. Check for output without result\n   359→    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n   360→    if output_path.exists():\n   361→        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n   362→            return INCOMPLETE\n   363→        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n   364→\n   365→    # 4. No output at all\n   366→    return ERROR\n   367→```\n   368→\n   369→## Integration Patterns\n   370→\n   371→### main.py Registration\n   372→\n   373→```python\n   374→# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\n   375→from superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\n   376→app.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n   377→```\n   378→\n   379→### Click Command Group\n   380→\n   381→```python\n   382→@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\n   383→def my_pipeline_group():\n   384→    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n   385→    pass\n   386→\n   387→@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n   388→@click.argument(\"source\")\n   389→@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n   390→@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n   391→@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n   392→@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n   393→@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\n   394→def run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n   395→    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n   396→    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n   397→    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n   398→    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n   399→```\n   400→"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":"toolu_01ARrV4zNqqgtQKuPjmHQfkE","session_id":"6d48e8db-6652-4750-84bd-06ac42d65350","uuid":"6c7631d7-7992-49da-bcd8-57d909dbec05"}

The command parses arguments, validates inputs, derives the output directory, and invokes the `sc:tasklist-protocol` skill which contains the full generation algorithm. The command itself does not execute any generation logic.\n    31→\n    32→## Arguments\n    33→\n    34→| Argument | Required | Default | Description |\n    35→|----------|----------|---------|-------------|\n    36→| `<roadmap-path>` | Yes | -- | Path to roadmap file. If the roadmap text contains a substring matching `.dev/releases/current/<segment>/` (first match), use that as `TASKLIST_ROOT`.\n    45→2. Else if the roadmap text contains a version token matching `v<digits>(.<digits>)+` (first match), set `TASKLIST_ROOT = .dev/releases/current/<version-token>/`.\n    46→3. Else fallback: `TASKLIST_ROOT = .dev/releases/current/v0.0-unknown/`.\n    47→\n    48→## Input Validation\n    49→\n    50→Before invoking the skill, the command validates all inputs. On any validation failure, the command emits an error and exits without invoking the skill. No partial output is written.\n    51→\n    52→**Error format** (2 fields):\n    53→```\n    54→error_code: <category string>\n    55→message: <human-readable description with corrective action>\n    56→```\n    57→\n    58→**Validation checks:**\n    59→\n    60→1. **Roadmap file exists and is readable**: `<roadmap-path>` resolves to a readable, non-empty file. Reject 0-byte or whitespace-only files.\n    61→   - Error: `error_code: EMPTY_INPUT` / `error_code: MISSING_FILE`\n    62→2. **Spec file exists (if provided)**: `--spec` path resolves to a readable file.\n    63→   - Error: `error_code: MISSING_FILE`\n    64→3. **Output parent directory exists (if provided)**: `--output` parent directory exists and is writable.\n    65→   - Error: `error_code: MISSING_FILE`\n    66→4. **TASKLIST_ROOT derivation succeeds (if --output not provided)**: The 3-step derivation algorithm produces a valid path.\n    67→   - This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n\n## Step Graph Design\n\n### Step Definition Pattern\n\nEvery workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n\n```python\nStep(\n    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n)\n```\n\n### Gate Mode Selection\n\nChoose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n\nRule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n- Milestone scope → configurable\n- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n\n### Parallel Group Pattern\n\nSteps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n\n```python\nsteps = [\n    single_step_1,\n    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n]\n```\n\nThe generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n\n### Dependency Rules\n\n- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n\n## Model Design Patterns\n\n### Config Model\n\nAlways extend `PipelineConfig`:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    # Required: identify the input\n    source_path: Path\n\n    # Optional: control behavior\n    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n\n    # Computed paths\n    @property\n    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n```\n\n### Status Enum\n\nSprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n\n```python\nclass StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n```\n\n### Result Model\n\nExtend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyStepResult(StepResult):\n    exit_code: int | None = None\n    started_at: float | None = None\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    error_bytes: int = 0\n    # Domain-specific fields:\n    artifacts_produced: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    gate_details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\n### Monitor State\n\nDomain-specific signals extracted from NDJSON output:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyMonitorState:\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    # Domain-specific signals:\n    last_step_id: str | None = None\n    current_artifact: str | None = None\n    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n```\n\n## Gate Design Patterns\n\n### Gate Criteria Tiers\n\n```python\n# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\nEXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"exempt\")\n\n# Light: file exists and non-empty\nLIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"light\")\n\n# Standard: structural validation\nSTANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    tier=\"standard\",\n    min_lines=50,\n    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n)\n\n# Strict: structural + semantic validation\nSTRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    tier=\"strict\",\n    min_lines=100,\n    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(name=\"no_heading_gaps\", fn=_no_heading_gaps),\n        SemanticCheck(name=\"refs_resolve\", fn=_cross_refs_resolve),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n### Semantic Check Functions\n\nSemantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n\n```python\ndef _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n    # ... implementation ...\n    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n\ndef _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n    missing = required - present\n    if missing:\n        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n    return (True, \"\")\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Validation\n\nThe shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Diff Analysis\nstatus: complete\ndiff_points: 12\nconvergence_ready: true\n---\n```\n\n## Prompt Design Patterns\n\n### Prompt Builder Structure\n\nEach step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n\n```python\ndef build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n\nSource: {source_path}\nDepth: {config.depth}\n\n## Required Output Format\n\nWrite your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Analysis Report\nstatus: complete\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Summary\nBrief overview of findings.\n\n### Findings\nNumbered list of findings with evidence.\n\n### Recommendations\nActionable next steps.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nAt the end of your output, include:\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n```\nor\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n```\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### Key Prompt Rules\n\n1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n\n### Input Embedding Pattern\n\n```python\ndef _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n    file_args = []\n    for input_path in inputs:\n        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n            content = full_path.read_text()\n            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n        else:\n            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n    return prompt, file_args\n```\n\n## Executor Design Patterns\n\n### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n\nThe sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = MyLogger(config)\n    tui = MyTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = MyResult(config=config)\n    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n\n    # 3. Start TUI\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in config.steps:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                break\n\n            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n            process.start()\n\n            # 6. Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall detection\n                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                # TUI update\n                tui.update(step, state)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # 7. Classify result\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n\n            # 8. Record and decide\n            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n            result.add(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n                result.outcome = HALTED\n                break\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        signal_handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n```\n\n### Status Classification\n\nMap every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n\n```python\ndef determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n    # 1. Hard failures\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return ERROR\n\n    # 2. Check for structured result file\n    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return PASS\n        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    # 3. Check for output without result\n    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return INCOMPLETE\n        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    # 4. No output at all\n    return ERROR\n```\n\n## Integration Patterns\n\n### main.py Registration\n\n```python\n# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\nfrom superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\napp.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n```\n\n### Click Command Group\n\n```python\n@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\ndef my_pipeline_group():\n    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n@click.argument(\"source\")\n@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\ndef run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n```\n\n## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n\nFor pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    max_turns: int = 200\n    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n\n# In executor:\nledger = TurnLedger(\n    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n)\n\n# Before launching a step:\nif not ledger.can_launch():\n    result.outcome = HALTED\n    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n    break\n\n# After step completes, count actual turns used:\nactual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\nledger.debit(actual_turns)\n\n# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\nif actual_turns < allocated:\n    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n```\n\n## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n\nFor pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n\n```python\ndef setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n    env = os.environ.copy()\n\n    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n\n    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n\n    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n\n    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n\n    return env\n```\n\n## Context Injection Pattern\n\nPrior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n\n```python\ndef build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n    base_prompt = step.prompt\n\n    if not prior_results:\n        return base_prompt\n\n    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n\n    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n```\n\n## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n\nOn halt, generate actionable resume information:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyResult:\n    # ... other fields ...\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n        if not self.halt_step:\n            return None\n        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n        return (\n            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n```\n\n## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n\nNot all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n\n```python\ndef execute_step(step, config):\n    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n    if step.prompt == \"\":\n        # Pure programmatic — run directly\n        return run_programmatic_step(step, config)\n    else:\n        # Claude-assisted — launch subprocess\n        return run_claude_step(step, config)\n\ndef run_programmatic_step(step, config) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a pure-programmatic step without Claude.\"\"\"\n    started = time.time()\n    try:\n        # Call the step's implementation function\n        PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS[step.id](config)\n        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n    except Exception as e:\n        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n                         gate_failure_reason=str(e),\n                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n```\n\n## Gate Display State Machine (for TUI)\n\nModel gate states as explicit transitions for richer UX:\n\n```python\nclass GateDisplayState(Enum):\n    NONE = \"none\"\n    CHECKING = \"checking\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    FAIL_DEFERRED = \"fail_deferred\"\n    REMEDIATING = \"remediating\"\n    REMEDIATED = \"remediated\"\n    HALT = \"halt\"\n\n    @property\n    def icon(self) -> str:\n        return {\n            \"none\": \" \", \"checking\": \"...\",\n            \"pass\": \"ok\", \"fail_deferred\": \"!\",\n            \"remediating\": \"~\", \"remediated\": \"ok\",\n            \"halt\": \"X\",\n        }[self.value]\n```\n```\n\n### C. `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.venv/lib/python3.12/site-packages/superclaude/_src/superclaude/skills/sc-cli-portify/refs/pipeline-spec.md`\n\nThis copy is similar but not identical.\n\n```md\n# Pipeline Specification Reference\n\nLoaded during Phase 2 of portification. This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n\n## Step Graph Design\n\n### Step Definition Pattern\n\nEvery workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n\n```python\nStep(\n    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n)\n```\n\n### Parallel Group Pattern\n\nSteps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n\n```python\nsteps = [\n    single_step_1,\n    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n]\n```\n\nThe generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Diff Analysis\nstatus: complete\ndiff_points: 12\nconvergence_ready: true\n---\n```\n\n## Prompt Design Patterns\n\n### Prompt Builder Structure\n\nEach step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n\n```python\ndef build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n\nSource: {source_path}\nDepth: {config.depth}\n\n## Required Output Format\n\nWrite your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Analysis Report\nstatus: complete\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Summary\nBrief overview of findings.\n\n### Findings\nNumbered list of findings with evidence.\n\n### Recommendations\nActionable next steps.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nAt the end of your output, include:\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n```\nor\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n```\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### Key Prompt Rules\n\n1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt;
