Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = MyLogger(config)\n    tui = MyTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = MyResult(config=config)\n\n    # 3. Start TUI\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in config.steps:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                break\n\n            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n            process.start()\n\n            # 6. Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall detection\n                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                # TUI update\n                tui.update(step, state)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # 7. Classify result\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n\n            # 8. Record and decide\n            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n            result.add(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n                result.outcome = HALTED\n                break\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        signal_handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n```\n\n### Status Classification\n\nMap every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n\n```python\ndef determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n    # 1. Hard failures\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return ERROR\n\n    # 2. Check for structured result file\n    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return PASS\n        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    # 3. Check for output without result\n    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return INCOMPLETE\n        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    # 4. No output at all\n    return ERROR\n```\n\n## Integration Patterns\n\n### main.py Registration\n\n```python\n# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\nfrom superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\napp.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n```\n\n### Click Command Group\n\n```python\n@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\ndef my_pipeline_group():\n    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n@click.argument(\"source\")\n@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\ndef run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n```\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2) `refs/code-templates.md` — full contents\n\n### A. `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/skills/sc-cli-portify/refs/code-templates.md`\n### B. `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.claude/skills/sc-cli-portify/refs/code-templates.md`\n\nThese two copies are identical.\n\n```md\n# Code Templates Reference\n\nLoaded during Phase 3 of portification. Contains the actual file templates used to generate each module in the CLI pipeline package.\n\nThese templates are parameterized. Placeholders use `{PARAM}` syntax. The skill fills these based on the pipeline specification from Phase 2.\n\n## File Generation Order\n\nGenerate in this order to respect dependencies:\n\n1. `models.py` — No internal deps\n2. `gates.py` — Imports from models\n3. `prompts.py` — Imports from models\n4. `config.py` — Imports from models\n5. `monitor.py` — Imports from models\n6. `process.py` — Imports from models, config; extends pipeline.process\n7. `executor.py` — Imports from everything above\n8. `tui.py` — Imports from models\n9. `logging_.py` — Imports from models\n10. `diagnostics.py` — Imports from models\n11. `commands.py` — Imports from config, executor\n12. `__init__.py` — Re-exports\n\n## Template: `__init__.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"CLI subcommand package for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nPortified from: {SOURCE_SKILL}\nGenerated by: sc-cli-portify\n\nThis module provides the `superclaude {CLI_NAME}` command group.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom .commands import {GROUP_NAME}_group\n\n__all__ = [\"{GROUP_NAME}_group\"]\n```\n\n## Template: `models.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Domain models for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nExtends shared pipeline base types with {PIPELINE_NAME}-specific\nstatus tracking, configuration, and result telemetry.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport time\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Any\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.pipeline.models import (\n    GateCriteria,\n    GateMode,\n    PipelineConfig,\n    Step,\n    StepResult,\n    StepStatus,\n)\n\n\n# --- Enums ---\n\nclass {PREFIX}Status(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Step-level status for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\n    Extends generic StepStatus with domain-specific states.\n    \"\"\"\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"\n    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"\n    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"\n    HALT = \"halt\"\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"\n    ERROR = \"error\"\n    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"\n\n\nclass {PREFIX}Outcome(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Aggregate pipeline outcome.\"\"\"\n    SUCCESS = \"success\"\n    HALTED = \"halted\"\n    INTERRUPTED = \"interrupted\"\n    ERROR = \"error\"\n\n\n{DOMAIN_ENUMS}\n\n\n# --- Configuration ---\n\n@dataclass\nclass {PREFIX}Config(PipelineConfig):\n    \"\"\"{PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline configuration.\n\n    Extends PipelineConfig with {PIPELINE_NAME}-specific settings.\n    \"\"\"\n    {CONFIG_FIELDS}\n\n    def __post_init__(self):\n        \"\"\"Ensure work_dir is set from pipeline-specific paths.\"\"\"\n        if not self.work_dir:\n            self.work_dir = self.{PRIMARY_PATH_FIELD}\n        self.work_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n\n    {CONFIG_PROPERTIES}\n\n\n# --- Step Specialization ---\n\n@dataclass\nclass {PREFIX}Step(Step):\n    \"\"\"{PIPELINE_NAME}-specific step with domain metadata.\"\"\"\n    {STEP_FIELDS}\n\n\n# --- Result Types ---\n\n@dataclass\nclass {PREFIX}StepResult(StepResult):\n    \"\"\"Result for a single {PIPELINE_NAME} step.\n\n    Extends StepResult with execution telemetry.\n    \"\"\"\n    status: {PREFIX}Status = {PREFIX}Status.PENDING\n    exit_code: int | None = None\n    started_at: float | None = None\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    error_bytes: int = 0\n    {RESULT_FIELDS}\n\n    @property\n    def duration_seconds(self) -> float:\n        if self.started_at and self.finished_at:\n            return self.finished_at - self.started_at\n        return 0.0\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass {PREFIX}Result:\n    \"\"\"Aggregate result for the entire {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config: {PREFIX}Config\n    step_results: list[{PREFIX}StepResult] = field(default_factory=list)\n    outcome: {PREFIX}Outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.SUCCESS\n    started_at: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    halt_step: str | None = None\n\n    @property\n    def duration_seconds(self) -> float:\n        end = self.finished_at or time.time()\n        return end - self.started_at\n\n    @property\n    def steps_passed(self) -> int:\n        return sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                   if r.status in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL))\n\n    @property\n    def steps_failed(self) -> int:\n        return sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                   if r.status in ({PREFIX}Status.HALT, {PREFIX}Status.ERROR, {PREFIX}Status.TIMEOUT))\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from the failed step.\"\"\"\n        if self.halt_step:\n            return f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run --resume --start {self.halt_step}\"\n        return None\n\n\n# --- Monitor State ---\n\n@dataclass\nclass {PREFIX}MonitorState:\n    \"\"\"Live execution state fed by the output monitor.\"\"\"\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    output_bytes_prev: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    last_event_time: float = 0.0\n    step_started_at: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    {MONITOR_FIELDS}\n\n    @property\n    def stall_status(self) -> str:\n        if self.events_received == 0:\n            elapsed = time.time() - self.step_started_at if self.step_started_at else 0\n            return \"waiting...\" if elapsed < 30 else \"STALLED\"\n        if self.stall_seconds > 120:\n            return \"STALLED\"\n        if self.stall_seconds > 30:\n            return \"thinking...\"\n        return \"active\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_size_display(self) -> str:\n        if self.output_bytes < 1024:\n            return f\"{self.output_bytes}B\"\n        return f\"{self.output_bytes / 1024:.1f}KB\"\n```\n\n## Template: `gates.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Gate criteria and semantic checks for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nEach step's output must pass its gate before the pipeline continues.\nGates enforce structural and semantic quality programmatically,\nremoving this responsibility from inference.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nimport yaml\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.pipeline.models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\n\n\n# --- Semantic Check Functions ---\n# Pure functions: (content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]\n\n{SEMANTIC_CHECKS}\n\n\n# --- Gate Definitions ---\n\n{GATE_DEFINITIONS}\n\n# Collected for iteration\nALL_GATES: dict[str, GateCriteria] = {{\n    {GATE_DICT_ENTRIES}\n}}\n```\n\n## Template: `prompts.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Prompt builders for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nEach function constructs the LLM contract for one pipeline step.\nThe prompt specifies:\n- What context/inputs to read\n- What output format is required\n- What machine-readable markers must appear\n- What quality expectations apply\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import {PREFIX}Config\n\n{DEPTH_INSTRUCTIONS}\n\n{PROMPT_BUILDERS}\n```\n\n## Template: `config.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Configuration loading and validation for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nHandles CLI argument resolution, file discovery, and config construction.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import {PREFIX}Config\n\n{CONFIG_CONSTANTS}\n\n\ndef load_{CLI_NAME}_config(\n    {CONFIG_PARAMS}\n) -> {PREFIX}Config:\n    \"\"\"Construct and validate pipeline configuration from CLI arguments.\"\"\"\n    {CONFIG_BODY}\n    return config\n\n\n{CONFIG_HELPERS}\n```\n\n## Template: `executor.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Sprint-style supervised executor for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nControls the execution loop with:\n- Per-step live monitoring\n- TUI refresh at ~2Hz\n- Stall detection and watchdog\n- Signal-aware graceful shutdown\n- Deterministic status classification\n- Failure diagnostics\n\nIMPORTANT: Use synchronous execution with threading, NOT async/await.\nSprint uses time.sleep() polling loops and concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor\nfor parallel batch dispatch. Do not use asyncio.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport shutil\nimport signal\nimport sys\nimport time\nfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\nfrom .config import load_{CLI_NAME}_config\nfrom .diagnostics import DiagnosticCollector, FailureClassifier, ReportGenerator\nfrom .logging_ import {PREFIX}Logger\nfrom .models import (\n    {PREFIX}Config,\n    {PREFIX}MonitorState,\n    {PREFIX}Outcome,\n    {PREFIX}Result,\n    {PREFIX}Status,\n    {PREFIX}StepResult,\n)\nfrom .monitor import OutputMonitor, detect_error_max_turns\nfrom .process import {PREFIX}Process, SignalHandler\nfrom .tui import {PREFIX}TUI\n\n\ndef execute_{CLI_NAME}(config: {PREFIX}Config) -> {PREFIX}Result:\n    \"\"\"Execute the {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline with supervised monitoring.\"\"\"\n\n    # Pre-flight\n    if not shutil.which(\"claude\"):\n        print(\"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Setup infrastructure\n    handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = {PREFIX}Logger(config)\n    tui = {PREFIX}TUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = {PREFIX}Result(config=config)\n\n    logger.write_header()\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in _build_steps(config):\n            if handler.shutdown_requested:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Reset monitor for this step's output\n            output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Launch subprocess\n            process = {PREFIX}Process(config, step)\n            logger.write_step_start(step)\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + step.timeout_seconds\n            process.start()\n\n            # Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall watchdog\n                if (config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.events_received > 0):\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        process.stop()\n                        break\n\n                try:\n                    tui.update(step, state)\n                except Exception:\n                    pass\n\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # Classify result\n            exit_code = process.wait()\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = _determine_status(exit_code, step, config)\n\n            step_result = {PREFIX}StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=status,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=process.started_at,\n                finished_at=time.time(),\n                output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n            )\n            result.step_results.append(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            # Gate check for passing steps\n            if status == {PREFIX}Status.PASS and step.gate:\n                output_content = (config.work_dir / step.output_file).read_text()\n                passed, reason = gate_passed(output_content, step.gate)\n                if not passed:\n                    step_result.status = {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n                    step_result.gate_failure_reason = reason\n                    status = {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n\n            # Handle failures\n            if status not in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                collector = DiagnosticCollector()\n                bundle = collector.collect(step_result, monitor.state, config)\n                classifier = FailureClassifier()\n                category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n                reporter = ReportGenerator()\n                reporter.write_report(bundle, category, config)\n\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.HALTED\n                result.halt_step = step.id\n                break\n\n        # Finalize\n        if result.outcome == {PREFIX}Outcome.SUCCESS:\n            all_passed = all(\n                r.status in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT, {PREFIX}Status.SKIPPED)\n                for r in result.step_results\n            )\n            if not all_passed:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.ERROR\n\n        result.finished_at = time.time()\n        logger.write_summary(result)\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n\n\n{BUILD_STEPS_FUNCTION}\n\n\ndef _determine_status(\n    exit_code: int | None,\n    step,\n    config: {PREFIX}Config,\n) -> {PREFIX}Status:\n    \"\"\"Classify step outcome from exit code and output artifacts.\"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code and exit_code != 0:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n\n    result_path = config.work_dir / f\"{step.id}-result.md\"\n    output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: PASS\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: FAIL\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return {PREFIX}Status.INCOMPLETE\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n```\n\n## Template: `monitor.py`\n\nFollow the sprint monitor pattern exactly — incremental NDJSON tail with signal extraction. See `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/monitor.py` for the implementation. Adapt signal patterns for the domain.\n\n## Template: `process.py`\n\nFollow the sprint process pattern — subclass pipeline `ClaudeProcess`, specialize the constructor for domain config, and implement `build_prompt()` that constructs the step's prompt with proper `/sc:task-unified` framing. See `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/process.py`.\n\n## Template: `tui.py`\n\nFollow the sprint TUI pattern — Rich Live display with header, step table, progress bar, and active step panel. Adapt the status styles and display fields for the domain. See `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/tui.py`.\n\n## Template: `logging_.py`\n\nFollow the sprint logging pattern — dual JSONL + Markdown logging with screen output. See `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/logging_.py`.\n\n## Template: `diagnostics.py`\n\nFollow the sprint diagnostics pattern — `DiagnosticCollector`, `FailureClassifier`, `ReportGenerator`. Adapt failure categories for the domain. See `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/diagnostics.py`.\n\n## Template: `commands.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Click CLI commands for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nProvides the `superclaude {CLI_NAME}` command group.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport sys\n\nimport click\n\nfrom .config import load_{CLI_NAME}_config\nfrom .executor import execute_{CLI_NAME}\n\n\n@click.group(\"{CLI_NAME}\")\ndef {GROUP_NAME}_group():\n    \"\"\"{PIPELINE_DESCRIPTION}\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n\n@{GROUP_NAME}_group.command(\"run\")\n{CLICK_ARGUMENTS}\n{CLICK_OPTIONS}\ndef run({RUN_PARAMS}):\n    \"\"\"Execute the {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config = load_{CLI_NAME}_config({CONFIG_ARGS})\n\n    if dry_run:\n        _print_dry_run(config)\n        return\n\n    result = execute_{CLI_NAME}(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.outcome.value == \"success\" else 1)\n\n\ndef _print_dry_run(config):\n    \"\"\"Display execution plan without running.\"\"\"\n    from rich.console import Console\n    from rich.table import Table\n\n    console = Console()\n    table = Table(title=f\"{PIPELINE_NAME} Pipeline Plan\")\n    table.add_column(\"Step\", style=\"cyan\")\n    table.add_column(\"Output\", style=\"green\")\n    table.add_column(\"Gate\", style=\"yellow\")\n    table.add_column(\"Timeout\", style=\"dim\")\n\n    {DRY_RUN_ROWS}\n\n    console.print(table)\n```\n\n## Integration Template: `main.py` Patch\n\nAdd after the last existing import:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.{MODULE_NAME} import {GROUP_NAME}_group\n```\n\nAdd after the last existing `app.add_command()`:\n\n```python\napp.add_command({GROUP_NAME}_group)\n```\n```\n\n### C. `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.venv/lib/python3.12/site-packages/superclaude/_src/superclaude/skills/sc-cli-portify/refs/code-templates.md`\n\nThis copy is similar but differs in imports and executor guidance.\n\n```md\n# Code Templates Reference\n\nLoaded during Phase 3 of portification. {PREFIX}Status.ERROR, {PREFIX}Status.TIMEOUT))\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from the failed step.\"\"\"\n        if self.halt_step:\n            return f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run --resume --start {self.halt_step}\"\n        return None\n\n\n# --- Monitor State ---\n\n@dataclass\nclass {PREFIX}MonitorState:\n    \"\"\"Live execution state fed by the output monitor.\"\"\"\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    output_bytes_prev: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    last_event_time: float = 0.0\n    step_started_at: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    {MONITOR_FIELDS}\n\n    @property\n    def stall_status(self) -> str:\n        if self.events_received == 0:\n            elapsed = time.time() - self.step_started_at if self.step_started_at else 0\n            return \"waiting...\" if elapsed < 30 else \"STALLED\"\n        if self.stall_seconds > 120:\n            return \"STALLED\"\n        if self.stall_seconds > 30:\n            return \"thinking...\"\n        return \"active\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_size_display(self) -> str:\n        if self.output_bytes < 1024:\n            return f\"{self.output_bytes}B\"\n        return f\"{self.output_bytes / 1024:.1f}KB\"\n```\n\n## Template: {PREFIX}Result:\n    \"\"\"Execute the {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline with supervised monitoring.\"\"\"\n\n    # Pre-flight\n    if not shutil.which(\"claude\"):\n        print(\"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Setup infrastructure\n    handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = {PREFIX}Logger(config)\n    tui = {PREFIX}TUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = {PREFIX}Result(config=config)\n\n    logger.write_header()\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in _build_steps(config):\n            if handler.shutdown_requested:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Reset monitor for this step's output\n            output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Launch subprocess\n            process = {PREFIX}Process(config, step)\n            logger.write_step_start(step)\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + step.timeout_seconds\n            process.start()\n\n            # Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall watchdog\n                if (config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.events_received > 0):\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        process.stop()\n                        break\n\n                try:\n                    tui.update(step, state)\n                except Exception:\n                    pass\n\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # Classify result\n            exit_code = process.wait()\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = _determine_status(exit_code, step, config)\n\n            step_result = {PREFIX}StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=status,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=process.started_at,\n                finished_at=time.time(),\n                output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n            )\n            result.step_results.append(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            # Gate check for passing steps\n            if status == {PREFIX}Status.PASS and step.gate:\n                output_content = (config.work_dir / step.output_file).read_text()\n                passed, reason = gate_passed(output_content, step.gate)\n                if not passed:\n                    step_result.status = {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n                    step_result.gate_failure_reason = reason\n                    status = {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n\n            # Handle failures\n            if status not in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                collector = DiagnosticCollector()\n                bundle = collector.collect(step_result, monitor.state, config)\n                classifier = FailureClassifier()\n                category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n                reporter = ReportGenerator()\n                reporter.write_report(bundle, category, config)\n\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.HALTED\n                result.halt_step = step.id\n                break\n\n        # Finalize\n        if result.outcome == {PREFIX}Outcome.SUCCESS:\n            all_passed = all(\n                r.status in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT, {PREFIX}Status.SKIPPED)\n                for r in result.step_results\n            )\n            if not all_passed:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.ERROR\n\n        result.finished_at = time.time()\n        logger.write_summary(result)\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n\n\n{BUILD_STEPS_FUNCTION}\n\n\ndef _determine_status(\n    exit_code: int | None,\n    step,\n    config: {PREFIX}Config,\n) -> {PREFIX}Status:\n    \"\"\"Classify step outcome from exit code and output artifacts.\"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code and exit_code != 0:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n\n    result_path = config.work_dir / f\"{step.id}-result.md\"\n    output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: PASS\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: FAIL\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return {PREFIX}Status.INCOMPLETE\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n```\n\n## Template: `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/models.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Pipeline data models -- shared dataclasses consumed by sprint and roadmap.\n\nThis module has zero imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or\nsuperclaude.cli.roadmap (NFR-007). All types here are generic pipeline\nprimitives that both consumers extend.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Callable, Literal, Optional\n\n\nclass StepStatus(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Lifecycle status of a single pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    PENDING = \"PENDING\"\n    PASS = \"PASS\"\n    FAIL = \"FAIL\"\n    TIMEOUT = \"TIMEOUT\"\n    CANCELLED = \"CANCELLED\"\n    SKIPPED = \"SKIPPED\"\n\n    @property\n    def is_terminal(self) -> bool:\n        return self in (\n            StepStatus.PASS,\n            StepStatus.FAIL,\n            StepStatus.TIMEOUT,\n            StepStatus.CANCELLED,\n            StepStatus.SKIPPED,\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def is_success(self) -> bool:\n        return self == StepStatus.PASS\n\n    @property\n    def is_failure(self) -> bool:\n        return self in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)\n\n\nclass GateMode(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Gating behavior for pipeline steps.\n\n    BLOCKING: Step must pass before the next step can begin (default).\n    TRAILING: Step runs but does not block subsequent steps; failures\n              are evaluated after a grace period.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    BLOCKING = \"BLOCKING\"\n    TRAILING = \"TRAILING\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass SemanticCheck:\n    \"\"\"Pure Python check applied to file content. No LLM invocation.\"\"\"\n\n    name: str\n    check_fn: Callable[[str], bool]\n    failure_message: str\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass GateCriteria:\n    \"\"\"Defines what constitutes a passing output for a pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    required_frontmatter_fields: list[str]\n    min_lines: int\n    enforcement_tier: Literal[\"STRICT\", \"STANDARD\", \"LIGHT\", \"EXEMPT\"] = \"STANDARD\"\n    semantic_checks: list[SemanticCheck] | None = None\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Step:\n    \"\"\"A single pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    id: str\n    prompt: str\n    output_file: Path\n    gate: Optional[GateCriteria]\n    timeout_seconds: int\n    inputs: list[Path] = field(default_factory=list)\n    retry_limit: int = 1\n    model: str = \"\"\n    gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Outcome of executing a single pipeline step.\"\"\"\n\n    step: Optional[Step] = None\n    status: StepStatus = StepStatus.PENDING\n    attempt: int = 1\n    gate_failure_reason: str | None = None\n    started_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc))\n    finished_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(timezone.utc))\n\n    @property\n    def duration_seconds(self) -> float:\n        return (self.finished_at - self.started_at).total_seconds()\n\n\nclass DeliverableKind(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Classification of deliverable type for decomposition and analysis.\"\"\"\n\n    IMPLEMENT = \"implement\"\n    VERIFY = \"verify\"\n    INVARIANT_CHECK = \"invariant_check\"\n    FMEA_TEST = \"fmea_test\"\n    GUARD_TEST = \"guard_test\"\n    CONTRACT_TEST = \"contract_test\"\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_str(cls, value: str) -> DeliverableKind:\n        \"\"\"Parse a string into a DeliverableKind, raising ValueError on unknown.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return cls(value)\n        except ValueError:\n            valid = \", \".join(k.value for k in cls)\n            raise ValueError(\n                f\"Unknown deliverable kind: {value!r}. Valid kinds: {valid}\"\n            )\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Deliverable:\n    \"\"\"A single deliverable within a pipeline step or roadmap task.\n\n    Attributes:\n        id: Unique identifier (e.g. 'D-0001', 'D-0001.a').\n        description: Human-readable description of what this deliverable produces.\n        kind: Classification for decomposition passes. Defaults to 'implement'\n              for backward compatibility with pre-extension deliverables.\n        metadata: Attachment point for analytical passes (M2-M4). Defaults to\n                  empty dict. Round-trip serializable.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    id: str\n    description: str\n    kind: DeliverableKind = DeliverableKind.IMPLEMENT\n    metadata: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n    def to_dict(self) -> dict:\n        \"\"\"Serialize to a dict for JSON round-trip.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"id\": self.id,\n            \"description\": self.description,\n            \"kind\": self.kind.value,\n            \"metadata\": self.metadata,\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    def from_dict(cls, data: dict) -> Deliverable:\n        \"\"\"Deserialize from a dict. Pre-extension dicts without 'kind' default to 'implement'.\"\"\"\n        kind_str = data.get(\"kind\", \"implement\")\n        return cls(\n            id=data[\"id\"],\n            description=data[\"description\"],\n            kind=DeliverableKind.from_str(kind_str),\n            metadata=data.get(\"metadata\", {}),\n        )\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass PipelineConfig:\n    \"\"\"Configuration shared by both sprint and roadmap pipelines.\"\"\"\n\n    work_dir: Path = field(default_factory=lambda: Path(\".\"))\n    dry_run: bool = False\n    max_turns: int = 100\n    model: str = \"\"\n    permission_flag: str = \"--dangerously-skip-permissions\"\n    debug: bool = False\n    grace_period: int = 0\n```\n\n### `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/gates.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Pipeline gate validation -- pure Python, no subprocess, no LLM invocation.\n\nValidates step outputs against GateCriteria with tier-proportional checks:\n  EXEMPT  -> always passes\n  LIGHT   -> file exists + non-empty\n  STANDARD -> + min lines + YAML frontmatter fields\n  STRICT  -> + semantic checks (if defined)\n\nNFR-003: No subprocess import. NFR-007: No sprint/roadmap imports.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\n\n\ndef gate_passed(output_file: Path, criteria: GateCriteria) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Validate a step's output against its gate criteria.\n\n    Returns (True, None) on pass.\n    Returns (False, reason) on failure where reason is human-readable.\n    \"\"\"\n    tier = criteria.enforcement_tier\n\n    # EXEMPT: always passes\n    if tier == \"EXEMPT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must exist\n    if not output_file.exists():\n        return False, f\"File not found: {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT, STANDARD, STRICT: file must be non-empty\n    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if len(content.strip()) == 0:\n        return False, f\"File empty (0 bytes): {output_file}\"\n\n    # LIGHT stops here\n    if tier == \"LIGHT\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: minimum line count\n    lines = content.splitlines()\n    if len(lines) < criteria.min_lines:\n        return False, (\n            f\"Below minimum line count: {len(lines)} < {criteria.min_lines} \"\n            f\"in {output_file}\"\n        )\n\n    # STANDARD, STRICT: YAML frontmatter fields\n    if criteria.required_frontmatter_fields:\n        ok, reason = _check_frontmatter(content, criteria.required_frontmatter_fields, output_file)\n        if not ok:\n            return False, reason\n\n    # STANDARD stops here\n    if tier == \"STANDARD\":\n        return True, None\n\n    # STRICT: semantic checks\n    if criteria.semantic_checks:\n        for check in criteria.semantic_checks:\n            if not check.check_fn(content):\n                return False, f\"Semantic check '{check.name}' failed: {check.failure_message}\"\n\n    return True, None\n\n\n_FRONTMATTER_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"^---[ \\t]*\\n((?:[ \\t]*\\w[\\w\\s]*:.*\\n)+)---[ \\t]*$\",\n    re.MULTILINE,\n)\n\n\ndef _check_frontmatter(\n    content: str, required_fields: list[str], output_file: Path\n) -> tuple[bool, str | None]:\n    \"\"\"Extract and validate YAML frontmatter fields.\n\n    Uses regex with re.MULTILINE to discover frontmatter anywhere in the\n    document (not just byte 0), allowing conversational preamble before the\n    ``---`` delimiters.  Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n    \"\"\"\n    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n    if match is None:\n        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n\n    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n\n    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" in line:\n            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n            if key:\n                found_keys.add(key)\n\n    for field in required_fields:\n        if field not in found_keys:\n            return False, f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\"\n\n    return True, None\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4) Current `sc-cli-portify` directory — recursive file list\n\nDirectory:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/commands/tasklist.md`\n\n```md\n---\nname: tasklist\ndescription: \"Generate deterministic, Sprint CLI-compatible tasklist bundles from roadmaps\"\ncategory: utility\ncomplexity: high\nallowed-tools: Read, Glob, Grep, Write, Bash, TodoWrite, Skill\nmcp-servers: [sequential, context7]\npersonas: [analyzer, architect]\nversion: \"1.0.0\"\n---\n\n# /sc:tasklist\n\nGenerate a deterministic, Sprint CLI-compatible tasklist bundle from a roadmap file. Transforms roadmap items into phased, execution-ready task files with compliance tier classification and verification routing.\n\n## Triggers\n\nWhen the user requests roadmap-to-tasklist conversion, sprint planning from a roadmap, or tasklist generation for execution via `superclaude sprint run`.\n\n## Usage\n\n```text\n/sc:tasklist <roadmap-path> [--spec <spec-path>] [--output <output-dir>]\n```\n\nBoth `@file` syntax and explicit file paths are supported for `<roadmap-path>` and `--spec`.\n\n## Behavioral Summary\n\nTransforms a roadmap into a Sprint CLI-compatible multi-file tasklist bundle. The command parses arguments, validates inputs, derives the output directory, and invokes the `sc:tasklist-protocol` skill which contains the full generation algorithm. The command itself does not execute any generation logic.\n\n## Arguments\n\n| Argument | Required | Default | Description |\n|----------|----------|---------|-------------|\n| `<roadmap-path>` | Yes | -- | Path to roadmap file. Accepts `@file` reference or explicit path. |\n| `--spec <spec-path>` | No | -- | Supplementary spec/context file for additional generation context. |\n| `--output <output-dir>` | No | Auto-derived from roadmap `TASKLIST_ROOT` | Output directory for the tasklist bundle. |\n\n### TASKLIST_ROOT Auto-Derivation\n\nWhen `--output` is not provided, `TASKLIST_ROOT` is derived from the roadmap content using this 3-step priority algorithm:\n\n1. If the roadmap text contains a substring matching `.dev/releases/current/<segment>/` (first match), use that as `TASKLIST_ROOT`.\n2. Else if the roadmap text contains a version token matching `v<digits>(.<digits>)+` (first match), set `TASKLIST_ROOT = .dev/releases/current/<version-token>/`.\n3. Else fallback: `TASKLIST_ROOT = .dev/releases/current/v0.0-unknown/`.\n\n## Input Validation\n\nBefore invoking the skill, the command validates all inputs. On any validation failure, the command emits an error and exits without invoking the skill. No partial output is written.\n\n**Error format** (2 fields):\n```text\nerror_code: <category string>\nmessage: <human-readable description with corrective action>\n```\n\n**Validation checks:**\n\n1. **Roadmap file exists and is readable**: `<roadmap-path>` resolves to a readable, non-empty file. Reject 0-byte or whitespace-only files.\n   - Error: `error_code: EMPTY_INPUT` / `error_code: MISSING_FILE`\n2. **Spec file exists (if provided)**: `--spec` path resolves to a readable file.\n   - Error: `error_code: MISSING_FILE`\n3. **Output parent directory exists (if provided)**: `--output` parent directory exists and is writable.\n   - Error: `error_code: MISSING_FILE`\n4. **TASKLIST_ROOT derivation succeeds (if --output not provided)**: The 3-step derivation algorithm produces a valid path.\n   - Error: `error_code: DERIVATION_FAILED`\n\n## Activation\n\n**Classification**: STRICT -- multi-file generation operation with compliance tier integration.\n\n**MANDATORY**: Before executing any protocol steps, invoke:\n> Skill sc:tasklist-protocol\n\nPass the following context:\n- Roadmap text: full content of the roadmap file\n- Spec text (if provided): full content of the spec file\n- Output directory: resolved TASKLIST_ROOT path\n\nDo NOT attempt to generate the tasklist using only this command file.\nThe full generation algorithm is in the protocol skill.\n\n## Examples\n\n```bash\n# Basic: generate tasklist from a roadmap\n/sc:tasklist @.dev/releases/current/v2.0/roadmap.md\n\n# With supplementary spec context\n/sc:tasklist @roadmap.md --spec @specs/auth-system-prd.md\n\n# Explicit output directory\n/sc:tasklist @roadmap.md --output .dev/releases/current/v2.1/tasklist/\n\n# Full invocation with all options\n/sc:tasklist @.dev/releases/current/v3.0/roadmap.md --spec @specs/v3-prd.md --output .dev/releases/current/v3.0/tasklist/\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Parse and validate input arguments\n- Derive TASKLIST_ROOT from roadmap content\n- Invoke the skill with validated context\n- Report generated file paths on completion\n\n**Will Not:**\n- Execute the generation algorithm (that is the skill's job)\n- Modify source roadmap files\n- Run `superclaude sprint run` (output is compatible; invocation is separate)\n- Generate anything beyond the tasklist bundle\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7) `verify-sync` configuration — Makefile targets related to `verify-sync` and `sync-dev`\n\nSource:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/Makefile`\n\n```make\n# Sync src/superclaude/{skills,agents} → .claude/{skills,agents} for local dev\nsync-dev:\n\t@echo \"🔄 Syncing src/superclaude/ → .claude/ for local development...\"\n\t@mkdir -p .claude/skills .claude/agents\n\t@for skill_dir in src/superclaude/skills/*/; Merges orchestration capabilities with MCP compliance into a single coherent interface.\nallowed-tools: Read, Glob, Grep, Edit, Write, Bash, TodoWrite, Task\n---\n\n> **NOTE**: Classification has already been performed by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The classification header has already been emitted. Do NOT emit it again. This skill handles **execution only** for STANDARD and STRICT tier tasks.\n>\n> If for any reason no classification header was emitted before this skill was invoked, emit one now using ONLY the tier values STRICT, STANDARD, LIGHT, or EXEMPT (no other values are valid).\n\n# /sc:task-unified - Unified Task Execution with Compliance\n\n## Purpose\n\nUnified command that merges orchestration capabilities with MCP compliance enforcement. Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Proceed directly to execution based on the classified tier.\n\n**Reference** — the tier keyword tables (for context only, do not re-classify):\n- **STRICT**: security, authentication, database, migration, refactor, breaking change, encrypt, token, session, oauth\n- **EXEMPT**: explain, search, commit, push, plan, discuss, brainstorm\n- **LIGHT**: typo, comment, whitespace, lint, docstring, formatting, minor\n- **STANDARD**: implement, add, create, update, fix, build, modify, change (default)\n\n### 2. Confidence Display (Human-Readable)\n\nAfter the mandatory classification header, show a human-readable summary:\n\n```text\n**Tier: STANDARD** [████████░░] 80%\n\nClassified as STANDARD:\n- Keywords matched: add, implement\n- Confidence score: 0.78\n- Considered alternatives: STRICT (0.35)\n```\n\nIf confidence <70%, add prompt: \"⚠️ Low confidence. Override with: `--compliance [strict|standard|light|exempt]`\"\n\n**Note**: The machine-readable header (Section 0) is for telemetry/A/B testing. This human-readable display is for user understanding.\n\n### 3. Execution Phase\n\nExecute task according to tier requirements:\n\n**STRICT Execution**:\n1. Activate project (mcp__serena__activate_project)\n2. Verify git working directory clean (git status)\n3. Load codebase context (codebase-retrieval)\n4. Check relevant memories (list_memories -> read_memory)\n5. Identify all affected files and test files\n6. Make changes with full checklist\n7. Identify all files that import changed code\n8. Update all affected files\n9. Spawn verification agent (quality-engineer)\n10. Run comprehensive tests: `pytest [path] -v`\n11. Answer adversarial questions\n\n**STANDARD Execution**:\n1. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final check\n\n## Examples\n\n### STRICT Task\n```text\n/sc:task \"implement user authentication with JWT\"\n\n-> Classified as STRICT (security domain, authentication keyword)\n-> Full 6-category checklist enforced\n-> Verification agent spawned\n-> Adversarial questions answered\n```\n\n### STANDARD Task\n```text\n/sc:task \"add pagination to user list\"\n\n-> Classified as STANDARD (add keyword, typical feature)\n-> Context loaded before editing\n-> Downstream impacts checked\n-> Direct test execution\n```\n\n### LIGHT Task\n```text\n/sc:task \"fix typo in README\"\n\n-> Classified as LIGHT (trivial keyword, documentation path)\n-> Quick sanity check only\n-> No verification delay\n```\n\n### EXEMPT Task\n```text\n/sc:task \"explain how the auth flow works\"\n\n-> Classified as EXEMPT (explain pattern detected)\n-> Immediate execution\n-> No compliance overhead\n```\n\n### Override Example\n```text\n/sc:task \"update config file\" --compliance strict\n\n-> User override to STRICT regardless of classification\n-> Full verification enforced\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Classify tasks into appropriate compliance tiers\n- Enforce tier-appropriate verification requirements\n- Provide confidence scoring with rationale\n- Track feedback for continuous calibration\n- Support user overrides with justification\n\n**Will Not:**\n- Skip safety-critical verification for STRICT tasks\n- Apply STRICT overhead to genuinely trivial changes\n- Override user's explicit compliance choice\n- Proceed with <70% confidence without user confirmation\n\n## Success Criteria\n\n| Metric | Target | Measurement |\n|--------|--------|-------------|\n| Tier classification accuracy | >=80% | User feedback on appropriateness |\n| User confusion rate | <10% | \"Which command?\" questions eliminated |\n| Skip rate (--skip-compliance) | <12% | Override tracking |\n| Regression prevention | >=85% | Post-verification bug detection |\n| STRICT tier overhead | <25% | Execution telemetry |\n\n## Configuration References\n\n- Keywords: `config/tier-keywords.yaml`\n- Verification routing: `config/verification-routing.yaml`\n- Acceptance criteria: `config/tier-acceptance-criteria.yaml`\n- Circuit breakers: See MCP.md\n- Routing logic: See ORCHESTRATOR.md\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9) Roadmap file — full contents\n\nPath:\n- `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/.dev/releases/current/v2.18-cli-portify-v2/roadmap.md`\n\n```md\n---\nspec_source: \"refactoring-spec-cli-portify.md\"\ncomplexity_score: 0.92\nadversarial: true\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis roadmap delivers the refactoring of `sc-cli-portify` from a monolithic skill into a command/protocol split architecture with contract-driven phase boundaries, live API conformance checking, deterministic code generation with AST verification, and comprehensive failure routing with resume semantics.\n\n**Scope**: 70 requirements (52 functional, 18 non-functional) across 7 domains at enterprise complexity (0.92). The work produces a 5-phase portification pipeline that transforms SuperClaude skill/command/agent workflows into programmatic CLI pipelines with validated Python code generation.\n\n**Critical path**: Ref file remediation → Command/Protocol split → Contract schema definition → Phase 0-1 implementation → Phase 2 design → Phase 3-4 code generation and integration → Golden fixture validation.\n\n**Key architectural decisions**:\n- Contract-driven phase boundaries (YAML with versioned schemas) — phases are independently resumable\n- Live API snapshot with hash verification prevents drift-induced generation errors\n- Atomic generation with AST validation ensures no partial or broken output\n- 7 supported patterns only — explicit boundary prevents aspirational scope creep\n- Determinism validated against enumerated artifacts (`source_step_registry`, `step_mapping`, `module_plan`)\n\n**Open questions**: All 10 OQs must be resolved before Phase 2 implementation begins. No downstream work proceeds until refs match the live API.\n\n1. Read live `models.py` and `gates.py` to capture current API signatures\n2. Horizontal rules (``---`` with no ``key: value``\n    content) are rejected because the pattern requires at least one\n    ``key: value`` line between delimiters.\n    \"\"\"\n    match = _FRONTMATTER_RE.search(content)\n    if match is None:\n        return False, f\"YAML frontmatter not found in {output_file}\"\n\n    frontmatter_text = match.group(1)\n\n    # Extract keys from key: value lines\n    found_keys: set[str] = set()\n    for line in frontmatter_text.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" in line:\n            key = line.split(\":\", 1)[0].strip()\n            if key:\n                found_keys.add(key)\n\n    for field in required_fields:\n        if field not in found_keys:\n            return False, f\"Missing required frontmatter field '{field}' in {output_file}\"\n\n    return True, None\n","numLines":109,"startLine":1,"totalLines":109}}}

This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n     4→\n     5→## Step Graph Design\n     6→\n     7→### Step Definition Pattern\n     8→\n     9→Every workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n    10→\n    11→```python\n    12→Step(\n    13→    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    14→    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    15→    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    16→    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    17→    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    18→    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    19→    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    20→    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    21→    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n    22→)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→### Gate Mode Selection\n    26→\n    27→Choose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n    28→- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n    29→- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n    30→\n    31→Rule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n    32→- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n    33→- Milestone scope → configurable\n    34→- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n    35→\n    36→### Parallel Group Pattern\n    37→\n    38→Steps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n    39→\n    40→```python\n    41→steps = [\n    42→    single_step_1,\n    43→    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    44→    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n    45→]\n    46→```\n    47→\n    48→The generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n    49→\n    50→### Dependency Rules\n    51→\n    52→- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n    53→- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n    54→- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n    55→- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n    56→\n    57→## Model Design Patterns\n    58→\n    59→### Config Model\n    60→\n    61→Always extend `PipelineConfig`:\n    62→\n    63→```python\n    64→@dataclass\n    65→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    66→    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    67→    # Required: identify the input\n    68→    source_path: Path\n    69→\n    70→    # Optional: control behavior\n    71→    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n    72→\n    73→    # Computed paths\n    74→    @property\n    75→    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n    76→        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n    77→\n    78→    @property\n    79→    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n    80→        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n    81→```\n    82→\n    83→### Status Enum\n    84→\n    85→Sprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n    86→\n    87→```python\n    88→class StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    89→    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    90→    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    91→    PASS = \"pass\"\n    92→    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    93→    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    94→    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    95→    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    96→    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    97→    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    98→    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n    99→```\n   100→\n   101→### Result Model\n   102→\n   103→Extend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n   104→\n   105→```python\n   106→@dataclass\n   107→class MyStepResult(StepResult):\n   108→    exit_code: int | None = None\n   109→    started_at: float | None = None\n   110→    finished_at: float | None = None\n   111→    output_bytes: int = 0\n   112→    error_bytes: int = 0\n   113→    # Domain-specific signals:\n   132→    last_step_id: str | None = None\n   133→    current_artifact: str | None = None\n   134→    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n   135→```\n   136→\n   137→## Gate Design Patterns\n   138→\n   139→### Gate Criteria Tiers\n   140→\n   141→```python\n   142→# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\n   143→EXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"exempt\")\n   144→\n   145→# Light: file exists and non-empty\n   146→LIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"light\")\n   147→\n   148→# Standard: structural validation\n   149→STANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n   150→    tier=\"standard\",\n   151→    min_lines=50,\n   152→    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n   153→)\n   154→\n   155→# Strict: structural + semantic validation\n   156→STRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n   157→    tier=\"strict\",\n   158→    min_lines=100,\n   159→    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n   160→    semantic_checks=[\n   161→        SemanticCheck(name=\"no_heading_gaps\", fn=_no_heading_gaps),\n   162→        SemanticCheck(name=\"refs_resolve\", fn=_cross_refs_resolve),\n   163→    ],\n   164→)\n   165→```\n   166→\n   167→### Semantic Check Functions\n   168→\n   169→Semantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n   170→\n   171→```python\n   172→def _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   173→    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n   174→    # ... implementation ...\n   175→    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n   176→\n   177→def _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n   178→    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n   179→    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n   180→    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n   181→    missing = required - present\n   182→    if missing:\n   183→        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n   184→    return (True, \"\")\n   185→```\n   186→\n   187→### Frontmatter Validation\n   188→\n   189→The shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n   190→\n   191→```yaml\n   192→---\n   193→title: Diff Analysis\n   194→status: complete\n   195→diff_points: 12\n   196→convergence_ready: true\n   197→---\n   198→```\n   199→\n   200→## Prompt Design Patterns\n   201→\n   202→### Prompt Builder Structure\n   203→\n   204→Each step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n   205→\n   206→```python\n   207→def build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n   208→    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n   209→\n   210→Source: {source_path}\n   211→Depth: {config.depth}\n   212→\n   213→## Required Output Format\n   214→\n   215→Write your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n   216→\n   217→```yaml\n   218→---\n   219→title: Analysis Report\n   220→status: complete\n   221→finding_count: <integer>\n   222→---\n   223→```\n   224→\n   225→## Sections Required\n   226→\n   227→### Summary\n   228→Brief overview of findings.\n   229→\n   230→### Findings\n   231→Numbered list of findings with evidence.\n   232→\n   233→### Recommendations\n   234→Actionable next steps.\n   235→\n   236→## Machine-Readable Markers\n   237→\n   238→At the end of your output, include:\n   239→```\n   240→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n   241→```\n   242→or\n   243→```\n   244→EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n   245→```\n   246→\"\"\"\n   247→```\n   248→\n   249→### Key Prompt Rules\n   250→\n   251→1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n   252→2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n   253→3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n   254→4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n   255→5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n   256→\n   257→### Input Embedding Pattern\n   258→\n   259→```python\n   260→def _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n   261→    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n   262→    file_args = []\n   263→    for input_path in inputs:\n   264→        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n   265→        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n   266→            content = full_path.read_text()\n   267→            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n   268→        else:\n   269→            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n   270→    return prompt, file_args\n   271→```\n   272→\n   273→## Executor Design Patterns\n   274→\n   275→### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n   276→\n   277→The sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n   278→\n   279→```python\n   280→def execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n   281→    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n   282→    verify_claude_binary()\n   283→\n   284→    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n   285→    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n   286→    logger = MyLogger(config)\n   287→    tui = MyTUI(config)\n   288→    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n   289→    result = MyResult(config=config)\n   290→    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n   291→\n   292→    # 3. Start TUI\n   293→    tui.start()\n   294→\n   295→    try:\n   296→        for step in config.steps:\n   297→            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   298→                break\n   299→\n   300→            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n   301→            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n   302→            monitor.start()\n   303→\n   304→            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n   305→            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n   306→            process.start()\n   307→\n   308→            # 6. Supervision loop\n   309→            while process.is_running():\n   310→                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n   311→                    process.stop()\n   312→                    break\n   313→\n   314→                state = monitor.get_state()\n   315→\n   316→                # Stall detection\n   317→                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n   318→                    process.stop()\n   319→                    break\n   320→\n   321→                # TUI update\n   322→                tui.update(step, state)\n   323→                time.sleep(0.5)\n   324→\n   325→            # 7. Classify result\n   326→            monitor.stop()\n   327→            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n   328→\n   329→            # 8. Record and decide\n   330→            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n   331→            result.add(step_result)\n   332→            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n   333→\n   334→            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n   335→                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n   336→                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n   337→                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n   338→                result.outcome = HALTED\n   339→                break\n   340→\n   341→    finally:\n   342→        tui.stop()\n   343→        monitor.stop()\n   344→        signal_handler.restore()\n   345→\n   346→    return result\n   347→```\n   348→\n   349→### Status Classification\n   350→\n   351→Map every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n   352→\n   353→```python\n   354→def determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n   355→    # 1. Hard failures\n   356→    if exit_code == 124:\n   357→        return TIMEOUT\n   358→    if exit_code != 0:\n   359→        return ERROR\n   360→\n   361→    # 2. Check for structured result file\n   362→    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n   363→    if result_path.exists():\n   364→        content = result_path.read_text()\n   365→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n   366→            return HALT\n   367→        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n   368→            return PASS\n   369→        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n   370→\n   371→    # 3. Check for output without result\n   372→    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n   373→    if output_path.exists():\n   374→        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n   375→            return INCOMPLETE\n   376→        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n   377→\n   378→    # 4. No output at all\n   379→    return ERROR\n   380→```\n   381→\n   382→## Integration Patterns\n   383→\n   384→### main.py Registration\n   385→\n   386→```python\n   387→# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\n   388→from superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\n   389→app.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n   390→```\n   391→\n   392→### Click Command Group\n   393→\n 416→For pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n   417→\n   418→```python\n   419→from superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n   420→\n   421→@dataclass\n   422→class MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n   423→    max_turns: int = 200\n   424→    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n   425→    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n   426→\n   427→# In executor:\n   428→ledger = TurnLedger(\n   429→    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n   430→    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n   431→    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n   432→)\n   433→\n   434→# Before launching a step:\n   435→if not ledger.can_launch():\n   436→    result.outcome = HALTED\n   437→    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n   438→    break\n   439→\n   440→# After step completes, count actual turns used:\n   441→actual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\n   442→ledger.debit(actual_turns)\n   443→\n   444→# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\n   445→if actual_turns < allocated:\n   446→    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n   447→```\n   448→\n   449→## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n   450→\n   451→For pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n   452→\n   453→```python\n   454→def setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n   455→    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n   456→    env = os.environ.copy()\n   457→\n   458→    # Layer 1: 479→Prior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n   480→\n   481→```python\n   482→def build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n   483→    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n   484→    base_prompt = step.prompt\n   485→\n   486→    if not prior_results:\n   487→        return base_prompt\n   488→\n   489→    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n   490→    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n   491→        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n   492→        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n   493→\n   494→    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n   495→```\n   496→\n   497→## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n   498→\n   499→On halt, generate actionable resume information:\n   500→\n   501→```python\n   502→@dataclass\n   503→class MyResult:\n   504→    # ... other fields ...\n   505→\n   506→    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n   507→        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n   508→        if not self.halt_step:\n   509→            return None\n   510→        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n   511→                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n   512→        return (\n   513→            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n   514→            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n   515→            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n   516→        )\n   517→\n   518→    @property\n   519→    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n   520→        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n   521→        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n   522→                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n   523→        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n   524→```\n   525→\n   526→## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n   527→\n   528→Not all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n   529→\n   530→```python\n   531→def execute_step(step, config):\n   532→    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n   533→    if step.prompt == \"\":\n   534→        #
