This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n\n## Step Graph Design\n\n### Step Definition Pattern\n\nEvery workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n\n```python\nStep(\n    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n)\n```\n\n### Gate Mode Selection\n\nChoose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n\nRule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n- Milestone scope → configurable\n- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n\n### Parallel Group Pattern\n\nSteps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n\n```python\nsteps = [\n    single_step_1,\n    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n]\n```\n\nThe generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n\n### Dependency Rules\n\n- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n\n## Model Design Patterns\n\n### Config Model\n\nAlways extend `PipelineConfig`:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    # Required: identify the input\n    source_path: Path\n\n    # Optional: control behavior\n    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n\n    # Computed paths\n    @property\n    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n```\n\n### Status Enum\n\nSprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n\n```python\nclass StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n```\n\n### Result Model\n\nExtend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyStepResult(StepResult):\n    exit_code: int | None = None\n    started_at: float | None = None\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    error_bytes: int = 0\n    # Domain-specific fields:\n    artifacts_produced: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    gate_details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\n### Monitor State\n\nDomain-specific signals extracted from NDJSON output:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyMonitorState:\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    # Domain-specific signals:\n    last_step_id: str | None = None\n    current_artifact: str | None = None\n    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n```\n\n## Gate Design Patterns\n\n### Gate Criteria Tiers\n\n```python\n# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\nEXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"exempt\")\n\n# Light: file exists and non-empty\nLIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"light\")\n\n# Standard: structural validation\nSTANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    tier=\"standard\",\n    min_lines=50,\n    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n)\n\n# Strict: structural + semantic validation\nSTRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    tier=\"strict\",\n    min_lines=100,\n    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(name=\"no_heading_gaps\", fn=_no_heading_gaps),\n        SemanticCheck(name=\"refs_resolve\", fn=_cross_refs_resolve),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n### Semantic Check Functions\n\nSemantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n\n```python\ndef _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n    # ... implementation ...\n    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n\ndef _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n    missing = required - present\n    if missing:\n        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n    return (True, \"\")\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Validation\n\nThe shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Diff Analysis\nstatus: complete\ndiff_points: 12\nconvergence_ready: true\n---\n```\n\n## Prompt Design Patterns\n\n### Prompt Builder Structure\n\nEach step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n\n```python\ndef build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n\nSource: {source_path}\nDepth: {config.depth}\n\n## Required Output Format\n\nWrite your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Analysis Report\nstatus: complete\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Summary\nBrief overview of findings.\n\n### Findings\nNumbered list of findings with evidence.\n\n### Recommendations\nActionable next steps.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nAt the end of your output, include:\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n```\nor\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n```\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### Key Prompt Rules\n\n1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n\n### Input Embedding Pattern\n\n```python\ndef _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n    file_args = []\n    for input_path in inputs:\n        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n            content = full_path.read_text()\n            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n        else:\n            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n    return prompt, file_args\n```\n\n## Executor Design Patterns\n\n### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n\nThe sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = MyLogger(config)\n    tui = MyTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = MyResult(config=config)\n    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n\n    # 3. Start TUI\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in config.steps:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                break\n\n            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n            process.start()\n\n            # 6. Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall detection\n                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                # TUI update\n                tui.update(step, state)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # 7. Classify result\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n\n            # 8. Record and decide\n            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n            result.add(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n                result.outcome = HALTED\n                break\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        signal_handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n```\n\n### Status Classification\n\nMap every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n\n```python\ndef determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n    # 1. Hard failures\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return ERROR\n\n    # 2. Check for structured result file\n    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return PASS\n        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    # 3. Check for output without result\n    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return INCOMPLETE\n        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    # 4. No output at all\n    return ERROR\n```\n\n## Integration Patterns\n\n### main.py Registration\n\n```python\n# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\nfrom superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\napp.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n```\n\n### Click Command Group\n\n```python\n@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\ndef my_pipeline_group():\n    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n@click.argument(\"source\")\n@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", execute_pipeline(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n```\n\n## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n\nFor pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    max_turns: int = 200\n    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n\n# In executor:\nledger = TurnLedger(\n    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n)\n\n# Before launching a step:\nif not ledger.can_launch():\n    result.outcome = HALTED\n    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n    break\n\n# After step completes, count actual turns used:\nactual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\nledger.debit(actual_turns)\n\n# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\nif actual_turns < allocated:\n    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n```\n\n## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n\nFor pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n\n```python\ndef setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n    env = os.environ.copy()\n\n    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n\n    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n\n    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n\n    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n\n    return env\n```\n\n## Context Injection Pattern\n\nPrior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n\n```python\ndef build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n    base_prompt = step.prompt\n\n    if not prior_results:\n        return base_prompt\n\n    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n\n    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n```\n\n## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n\nOn halt, generate actionable resume information:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyResult:\n    # ... other fields ...\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n        if not self.halt_step:\n            return None\n --start {self.halt_step} \"\n            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n```\n\n## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n\nNot all steps need Claude. str:\n        if self.events_received == 0:\n            elapsed = time.time() - self.step_started_at if self.step_started_at else 0\n            return \"waiting...\" if elapsed < 30 else \"STALLED\"\n        if self.stall_seconds > 120:\n            return \"STALLED\"\n        if self.stall_seconds > 30:\n            return \"thinking...\"\n        return \"active\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_size_display(self) -> str:\n        if self.output_bytes < 1024:\n            return f\"{self.output_bytes}B\"\n        return f\"{self.output_bytes / 1024:.1f}KB\"\n```\n\n## Template: `gates.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Gate criteria and semantic checks for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nEach step's output must pass its gate before the pipeline continues.\nGates enforce structural and semantic quality programmatically,\nremoving this responsibility from inference.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport re\nimport yaml\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.pipeline.models import GateCriteria, SemanticCheck\n\n\n# --- Semantic Check Functions ---\n# Pure functions: (content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]\n\n{SEMANTIC_CHECKS}\n\n\n# --- Gate Definitions ---\n\n{GATE_DEFINITIONS}\n\n# Collected for iteration\nALL_GATES: dict[str, GateCriteria] = {{\n    {GATE_DICT_ENTRIES}\n}}\n```\n\n## Template: `prompts.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Prompt builders for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nEach function constructs the LLM contract for one pipeline step.\nThe prompt specifies:\n- What context/inputs to read\n- What output format is required\n- What machine-readable markers must appear\n- What quality expectations apply\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import {PREFIX}Config\n\n{DEPTH_INSTRUCTIONS}\n\n{PROMPT_BUILDERS}\n```\n\n## Template: `config.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Configuration loading and validation for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nHandles CLI argument resolution, file discovery, and config construction.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom .models import {PREFIX}Config\n\n{CONFIG_CONSTANTS}\n\n\ndef load_{CLI_NAME}_config(\n    {CONFIG_PARAMS}\n) -> {PREFIX}Config:\n    \"\"\"Construct and validate pipeline configuration from CLI arguments.\"\"\"\n    {CONFIG_BODY}\n    return config\n\n\n{CONFIG_HELPERS}\n```\n\n## Template: `executor.py`\n\n```python\n\"\"\"Sprint-style supervised executor for {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline.\n\nControls the execution loop with:\n- Per-step live monitoring\n- TUI refresh at ~2Hz\n- Stall detection and watchdog\n- Signal-aware graceful shutdown\n- Deterministic status classification\n- Failure diagnostics\n\nIMPORTANT: Use synchronous execution with threading, NOT async/await.\nSprint uses time.sleep() polling loops and concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor\nfor parallel batch dispatch. Do not use asyncio.\n\nSource workflow: {SOURCE_SKILL}\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport shutil\nimport signal\nimport sys\nimport time\nfrom concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nfrom superclaude.cli.pipeline.gates import gate_passed\n\nfrom .config import load_{CLI_NAME}_config\nfrom .diagnostics import DiagnosticCollector, FailureClassifier, ReportGenerator\nfrom .logging_ import {PREFIX}Logger\nfrom .models import (\n    {PREFIX}Config,\n    {PREFIX}MonitorState,\n    {PREFIX}Outcome,\n    {PREFIX}Result,\n    {PREFIX}Status,\n    {PREFIX}StepResult,\n)\nfrom .monitor import OutputMonitor, detect_error_max_turns\nfrom .process import {PREFIX}Process, SignalHandler\nfrom .tui import {PREFIX}TUI\n\n\ndef execute_{CLI_NAME}(config: {PREFIX}Config) -> {PREFIX}Result:\n    \"\"\"Execute the {PIPELINE_NAME} pipeline with supervised monitoring.\"\"\"\n\n    # Pre-flight\n    if not shutil.which(\"claude\"):\n        print(\"Error: 'claude' binary not found in PATH\", file=sys.stderr)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # Setup infrastructure\n    handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = {PREFIX}Logger(config)\n    tui = {PREFIX}TUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = {PREFIX}Result(config=config)\n\n    logger.write_header()\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in _build_steps(config):\n            if handler.shutdown_requested:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.INTERRUPTED\n                break\n\n            # Reset monitor for this step's output\n            output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Launch subprocess\n            process = {PREFIX}Process(config, step)\n            logger.write_step_start(step)\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + step.timeout_seconds\n            process.start()\n\n            # Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                if time.monotonic() > deadline:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall watchdog\n                if (config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.events_received > 0):\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        process.stop()\n                        break\n\n                try:\n                    tui.update(step, state)\n                except Exception:\n                    pass\n\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # Classify result\n            exit_code = process.wait()\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = _determine_status(exit_code, step, config)\n\n            step_result = {PREFIX}StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=status,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=process.started_at,\n                finished_at=time.time(),\n                output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n            )\n            result.step_results.append(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            # Gate check for passing steps\n            if status == {PREFIX}Status.PASS and step.gate:\n                output_content = (config.work_dir / step.output_file).read_text()\n                passed, reason = gate_passed(output_content, step.gate)\n                if not passed:\n                    step_result.status = {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n                    step_result.gate_failure_reason = reason\n                    status = {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n\n            # Handle failures\n            if status not in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT):\n                collector = DiagnosticCollector()\n                bundle = collector.collect(step_result, monitor.state, config)\n                classifier = FailureClassifier()\n                category = classifier.classify(bundle)\n                reporter = ReportGenerator()\n                reporter.write_report(bundle, category, config)\n\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.HALTED\n                result.halt_step = step.id\n                break\n\n        # Finalize\n        if result.outcome == {PREFIX}Outcome.SUCCESS:\n            all_passed = all(\n                r.status in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT, {PREFIX}Status.SKIPPED)\n                for r in result.step_results\n            )\n            if not all_passed:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.ERROR\n\n        result.finished_at = time.time()\n        logger.write_summary(result)\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n\n\n{BUILD_STEPS_FUNCTION}\n\n\ndef _determine_status(\n    exit_code: int | None,\n    step,\n    config: {PREFIX}Config,\n) -> {PREFIX}Status:\n    \"\"\"Classify step outcome from exit code and output artifacts.\"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code and exit_code != 0:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n\n    result_path = config.work_dir / f\"{step.id}-result.md\"\n    output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: PASS\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: FAIL\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return {PREFIX}Status.INCOMPLETE\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n```\n\n## Template: `monitor.py`\n\nFollow the sprint monitor pattern exactly — incremental NDJSON tail with signal extraction. See `src/superclaude/cli/sprint/monitor.py` for the implementation. \"refactoring-spec-cli-portify.md\"\ncomplexity_score: 0.92\nadversarial: true\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis roadmap delivers the refactoring of `sc-cli-portify` from a monolithic skill into a command/protocol split architecture with contract-driven phase boundaries, live API conformance checking, deterministic code generation with AST verification, and comprehensive failure routing with resume semantics.\n\n**Scope**: 70 requirements (52 functional, 18 non-functional) across 7 domains at enterprise complexity (0.92). The work produces a 5-phase portification pipeline that transforms SuperClaude skill/command/agent workflows into programmatic CLI pipelines with validated Python code generation.\n\n**Critical path**: Ref file remediation → Command/Protocol split → Contract schema definition → Phase 0-1 implementation → Phase 2 design → Phase 3-4 code generation and integration → Golden fixture validation.\n\n**Key architectural decisions**:\n- Contract-driven phase boundaries (YAML with versioned schemas) — phases are independently resumable\n- Live API snapshot with hash verification prevents drift-induced generation errors\n- Atomic generation with AST validation ensures no partial or broken output\n- 7 supported patterns only — explicit boundary prevents aspirational scope creep\n- Determinism validated against enumerated artifacts (`source_step_registry`, `step_mapping`, `module_plan`)\n\n**Open questions**: All 10 OQs must be resolved before Phase 2 implementation begins. OQ-002 (TurnLedger), OQ-003 (dry-run behavior), OQ-004 (integration schema), OQ-007 (approval gate mechanism), and OQ-008 (default output path) are blocking for design work.\n\n**Estimated delivery**: 14–19 working sessions (approximately 26–35 working days, assuming 1.5–2 sessions per day with review latency).\n\n---\n\n## Phase 1: Foundation and Prerequisite Remediation\n\n**Duration**: 2–3 sessions (~3–5 days)\n**Goal**: Eliminate known drift, establish the split architecture, resolve blocking open questions, define contract schema versioning policy\n\n### Milestone 1.1: Ref File API Alignment\n\nAddresses RISK-002 (ref file staleness) — the highest-priority prerequisite. No downstream work proceeds until refs match the live API.\n\n1. Read live `models.py` and `gates.py` to capture current API signatures\n2. Update `refs/pipeline-spec.md`:\n   - Fix tier casing: `tier=\"strict\"` → `enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\"`\n   - Align `GateCriteria` field names to match live dataclass\n   - Correct `SemanticCheck` contract: `Callable[[str], bool]` signature, not `tuple[bool, str]`\n3. Update `refs/code-templates.md`:\n   - Align all import paths to `superclaude.cli.pipeline.models` / `.gates`\n   - Fix gate template to use actual `GateCriteria` constructor fields\n   - Verify all 12 file templates reference correct base classes\n4. **Validation**: Diff ref files against live API — zero field name mismatches. Add stale-ref detector script that compares ref field names against live API signatures.\n\n**Requirements**: FR-048, NFR-003, NFR-018\n**Risks mitigated**: RISK-002\n\n### Milestone 1.2: Command/Protocol Split\n\nRuns in parallel with Milestone 1.1.\n\n1. Create `src/superclaude/commands/cli-portify.md` (thin command shim):\n   - Parse arguments: `--workflow`, `--name`, `--output`, `--dry-run`, `--skip-integration`\n   - Input validation with 6 error codes (MISSING_WORKFLOW, INVALID_PATH, AMBIGUOUS_PATH, OUTPUT_NOT_WRITABLE, NAME_COLLISION, DERIVATION_FAILED)\n   - Delegate to `Skill sc:cli-portify-protocol`\n3. Define contract schema versioning policy:\n   - Schema version field in contract header (e.g., `schema_version: \"1.0\"`)\n   - Backward-compatibility rules: additive fields allowed, field removal requires major version bump\n   - Version validation on contract read — reject incompatible versions with actionable error\n2. Define YAML contract common header schema:\n   ```yaml\n   schema_version: \"1.0\"\n   phase: <int>\n   status: \"passed\" | \"failed\" | \"skipped\"\n   timestamp: <ISO8601>\n   resume_checkpoint: <string>\n   validation_status: {blocking_passed: <int>, blocking_failed: <int>, advisory: [...]}\n   ```\n3. Define per-phase contract schemas (`portify-prerequisites.yaml`, `portify-analysis.yaml`, `portify-spec.yaml`, `portify-codegen.yaml`, `portify-integration.yaml`, return contract)\n4. Implement contract validation logic — next phase reads and validates incoming contract before proceeding\n5. Implement return contract structure (FR-043): status, failure_phase, failure_type, generated_files, counts, api_snapshot_hash, resume_command, warnings, phase_contracts\n6. Implement resume protocol (FR-052): read latest contract, validate completed phases, resume from failure point\n7. Validate resume semantics with a synthetic failure scenario before Phase 0 runs — proves contract mechanics work independently\n8. Define null-field policy: unreached fields explicitly set to `null`\n\n**Requirements**: FR-007, FR-008, FR-009, FR-043, FR-052, NFR-009, NFR-015, NFR-016\n\n### Milestone 2.2: Phase 0 — Prerequisites\n\n1. Deterministic, formula-based, structural | Python function, no Claude |\n| **Programmatic + Validation** | Structural check with semantic judgment | Python primary, Claude for edge cases |\n| **Claude-Assisted** | Content generation within structured format | Claude subprocess with gate validation |\n| **Pure Inference** | Creative, subjective, context-dependent | Claude subprocess with light gate |\n\n### Map to Pipeline Primitives\n\n| Workflow Concept | Pipeline Primitive |\n|-----------------|-------------------|\n| Sequential step | `Step` in step list |\n| Parallel operations | `list[Step]` parallel group |\n| Quality gate | `GateCriteria` on the Step |\n| Agent delegation | Prompt in `prompts.py` |\n| Scoring formula | Python function in `gates.py` or separate module |\n| Status decision | `_determine_status()` in `executor.py` |\n| Input validation | `config.py` validation logic |\n| Output format | Frontmatter requirements in gate + prompt |\n| Retry on failure | `retry_limit` on Step |\n| Skip on success | Resume logic in executor |\n\n## Analysis Output Format\n\nPhase 1 produces `portify-analysis.md` with this structure:\n\n```markdown\n---\nsource_skill: <skill-name>\nsource_command: <command-name>\nstep_count: <N>\nparallel_groups: <N>\ngate_count: <N>\nagent_count: <N>\ncomplexity: simple|moderate|high\n---\n\n# Portification Analysis: {workflow-name}\n\n## Source Components\n\n| Component | Path | Lines | Purpose |\n|-----------|------|-------|---------|\n| Command | ... | ... | ... |\n| Skill | ... | ... | ... |\n| Agent: ... | ... | ... | ... |\n| Ref: ... | ... | ... | ... |\n\n## Step Graph\n\n### Step 1: {name}\n- **Type**: pure-programmatic | claude-assisted | hybrid\n- **Inputs**: [list of input artifacts]\n- **Output**: artifact-name.md\n- **Gate**: exempt | light | standard | strict\n- **Agent**: none | agent-name\n- **Parallel**: yes (with step N) | no\n- **Timeout**: Ns\n- **Retry**: N attempts\n- **Notes**: any special considerations\n\n### Step 2: {name}\n...\n\n## Parallel Groups\n\n| Group | Steps | Rationale |\n|-------|-------|-----------|\n| 1 | step-2, step-3 | Independent variant generation |\n\n## Gates Summary\n\n| Step | Tier | Frontmatter | Min Lines | Semantic Checks |\n|------|------|-------------|-----------|-----------------|\n| ... | ... | ... | ... | ... |\n\n## Agent Delegation Map\n\n| Agent | Used In Steps | Parallel | Contract |\n|-------|--------------|----------|----------|\n| ... | ... | ... | ... |\n\n## Data Flow Diagram\n\n```\n[input] → step-1 → [artifact-1]\n                         ↓\n                    ┌─step-2─┐\n                    │         │ (parallel)\n                    └─step-3─┘\n                         ↓\n               [artifact-2, artifact-3]\n                         ↓\n                    step-4 → [final-output]\n```\n\n## Classification Summary\n\n| Category | Count | Steps |\n|----------|-------|-------|\n| Pure Programmatic | N | ... |\n| Claude-Assisted | N | ... |\n| Hybrid | N | ... |\n| Pure Inference | N | ... |\n\n## Recommendations\n\n- Things that should definitely be programmatic but are currently inference\n- Steps that could be split for better gate coverage\n- Opportunities for parallelization\n- Potential failure modes and how to handle them\n```\n\n## Common Workflow Patterns\n\n### Pattern: Multi-Agent Debate\nFound in: adversarial, spec-panel\n\nSteps:\n1. Parse inputs and validate (programmatic)\n2. Generate variants in parallel (Claude, parallel group)\n3. Diff analysis (Claude, single step with strict gate)\n4. Debate rounds (Claude, sequential with convergence gate)\n5. Score and select (hybrid — formulas are programmatic, rubrics are Claude)\n6. Generate plan (Claude, standard gate)\n7. Execute merge (Claude, strict gate with post-validation)\n\n### Pattern: Multi-Pass Audit\nFound in: cleanup-audit\n\nSteps:\n1. Discover files (programmatic)\n2. Surface scan with batching (Claude, batched parallel)\n3. Deep analysis per file (Claude, batched parallel)\n4. Cross-cutting comparison (Claude, single with strict gate)\n5. Consolidate findings (Claude, standard gate)\n6. Validate claims (Claude, sampling with standard gate)\n\n### Pattern: Extract-Transform-Validate\nFound in: roadmap, tasklist\n\nSteps:\n1. Extract requirements (Claude, strict gate on frontmatter)\n2. Generate artifacts (Claude, parallel for multiple agents)\n3. Compare/analyze (Claude, standard gate)\n4. Synthesize final (Claude, strict gate)\n5. Validate structure (programmatic)\n\n### Pattern: Iterative Refinement\nFound in: implement, improve\n\nSteps:\n1. Analyze current state (Claude, standard gate)\n2. Generate plan (Claude, standard gate)\n3. Execute changes (Claude, strict gate)\n4. Validate changes (programmatic + Claude)\n5. Iterate if quality threshold not met (retry loop)\n","numLines":216,"startLine":1,"totalLines":216}}}

This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n\n## Step Graph Design\n\n### Step Definition Pattern\n\nEvery workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n\n```python\nStep(\n    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n)\n```\n\n### Gate Mode Selection\n\nChoose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n\nRule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n- Milestone scope → configurable\n- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n\n### Parallel Group Pattern\n\nSteps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n\n```python\nsteps = [\n    single_step_1,\n    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n]\n```\n\nThe generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n\n### Dependency Rules\n\n- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n\n## Model Design Patterns\n\n### Config Model\n\nAlways extend `PipelineConfig`:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    # Required: identify the input\n    source_path: Path\n\n    # Optional: control behavior\n    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n\n    # Computed paths\n    @property\n    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n```\n\n### Status Enum\n\nSprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n\n```python\nclass StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n```\n\n### Result Model\n\nExtend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyStepResult(StepResult):\n    exit_code: int | None = None\n    started_at: float | None = None\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    error_bytes: int = 0\n    # Domain-specific fields:\n    artifacts_produced: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    gate_details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\n### Monitor State\n\nDomain-specific signals extracted from NDJSON output:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyMonitorState:\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    # Domain-specific signals:\n    last_step_id: str | None = None\n    current_artifact: str | None = None\n    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n```\n\n## Gate Design Patterns\n\n### Gate Criteria Tiers\n\n```python\n# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\nEXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"exempt\")\n\n# Light: file exists and non-empty\nLIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(tier=\"light\")\n\n# Standard: structural validation\nSTANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    tier=\"standard\",\n    min_lines=50,\n    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n)\n\n# Strict: structural + semantic validation\nSTRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    tier=\"strict\",\n    min_lines=100,\n    required_frontmatter=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(name=\"no_heading_gaps\", fn=_no_heading_gaps),\n        SemanticCheck(name=\"refs_resolve\", fn=_cross_refs_resolve),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n### Semantic Check Functions\n\nSemantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n\n```python\ndef _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n    # ... implementation ...\n    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n\ndef _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n    missing = required - present\n    if missing:\n        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n    return (True, \"\")\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Validation\n\nThe shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Diff Analysis\nstatus: complete\ndiff_points: 12\nconvergence_ready: true\n---\n```\n\n## Prompt Design Patterns\n\n### Prompt Builder Structure\n\nEach step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n\n```python\ndef build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n\nSource: {source_path}\nDepth: {config.depth}\n\n## Required Output Format\n\nWrite your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Analysis Report\nstatus: complete\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Summary\nBrief overview of findings.\n\n### Findings\nNumbered list of findings with evidence.\n\n### Recommendations\nActionable next steps.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nAt the end of your output, include:\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n```\nor\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n```\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### Key Prompt Rules\n\n1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n\n### Input Embedding Pattern\n\n```python\ndef _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n    file_args = []\n    for input_path in inputs:\n        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n            content = full_path.read_text()\n            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n        else:\n            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n    return prompt, file_args\n```\n\n## Executor Design Patterns\n\n### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n\nThe sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = MyLogger(config)\n    tui = MyTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = MyResult(config=config)\n    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n\n    # 3. Start TUI\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in config.steps:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                break\n\n            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n            process.start()\n\n            # 6. Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall detection\n                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                # TUI update\n                tui.update(step, state)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # 7. Classify result\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n\n            # 8. Record and decide\n            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n            result.add(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n                result.outcome = HALTED\n                break\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        signal_handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n```\n\n### Status Classification\n\nMap every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n\n```python\ndef determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n    # 1. Hard failures\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return ERROR\n\n    # 2. Check for structured result file\n    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return PASS\n        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    # 3. Check for output without result\n    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return INCOMPLETE\n        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    # 4. No output at all\n    return ERROR\n```\n\n## Integration Patterns\n\n### main.py Registration\n\n```python\n# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\nfrom superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\napp.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n```\n\n### Click Command Group\n\n```python\n@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\ndef my_pipeline_group():\n    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n@click.argument(\"source\")\n@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\ndef run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n```\n\n## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n\nFor pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    max_turns: int = 200\n    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n\n# In executor:\nledger = TurnLedger(\n    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n)\n\n# Before launching a step:\nif not ledger.can_launch():\n    result.outcome = HALTED\n    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n    break\n\n# After step completes, count actual turns used:\nactual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\nledger.debit(actual_turns)\n\n# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\nif actual_turns < allocated:\n    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n```\n\n## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n\nFor pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n\n```python\ndef setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n    env = os.environ.copy()\n\n    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n\n    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n\n    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n\n    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n\n    return env\n```\n\n## Context Injection Pattern\n\nPrior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n\n```python\ndef build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n    base_prompt = step.prompt\n\n    if not prior_results:\n        return base_prompt\n\n    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n\n    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n```\n\n## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n\nOn halt, generate actionable resume information:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyResult:\n    # ... other fields ...\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n        if not self.halt_step:\n            return None\n        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n        return (\n            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n```\n\n## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n\nNot all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n\n```python\ndef execute_step(step, config):\n    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n    if step.prompt == \"\":\n        # Pure programmatic — run directly\n        return run_programmatic_step(step, config)\n    else:\n        # Claude-assisted — launch subprocess\n        return run_claude_step(step, config)\n\ndef run_programmatic_step(step, config) -> StepResult:\n    \"\"\"Execute a pure-programmatic step without Claude.\"\"\"\n    started = time.time()\n    try:\n        # Call the step's implementation function\n        PROGRAMMATIC_RUNNERS[step.id](config)\n        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.PASS,\n                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n    except Exception as e:\n        return StepResult(step=step, status=StepStatus.FAIL,\n                         gate_failure_reason=str(e),\n                         started_at=started, finished_at=time.time())\n```\n\n## Gate Display State Machine (for TUI)\n\nModel gate states as explicit transitions for richer UX:\n\n```python\nclass GateDisplayState(Enum):\n    NONE = \"none\"\n    CHECKING = \"checking\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    FAIL_DEFERRED = \"fail_deferred\"\n    REMEDIATING = \"remediating\"\n    REMEDIATED = \"remediated\"\n    HALT = \"halt\"\n\n    @property\n    def icon(self) -> str:\n        return {\n            \"none\": \" \", \"checking\": \"...\",\n            \"pass\": \"ok\", \"fail_deferred\": \"!\",\n            \"remediating\": \"~\", \"remediated\": \"ok\",\n            \"halt\": \"X\",\n        }[self.value]\n```\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":140,"oldLines":26,"newStart":140,"newLines":42,"lines":[" "," ```python"," # This ref provides the detailed specification patterns for converting a workflow analysis into concrete code designs.\n\n## Step Graph Design\n\n### Step Definition Pattern\n\nEvery workflow operation that produces an artifact maps to a `Step`:\n\n```python\nStep(\n    id=\"step-id\",              # kebab-case, unique within pipeline\n    prompt=build_X_prompt(),   # Function from prompts.py\n    output_file=\"artifact.md\", # Relative to work_dir\n    gate=STEP_GATE,            # From gates.py\n    gate_mode=GateMode.BLOCKING,  # BLOCKING (default) or TRAILING\n    timeout_seconds=600,       # Per-step timeout\n    inputs=[\"dep1.md\"],        # Files this step reads\n    retry_limit=1,             # How many retries on gate failure\n    model=None,                # None = use default from config\n)\n```\n\n### Gate Mode Selection\n\nChoose `GateMode` based on step criticality:\n- `BLOCKING` (default): Pipeline halts if gate fails. Use for steps whose output is consumed by downstream steps.\n- `TRAILING`: Gate evaluates asynchronously; pipeline continues. Use for quality checks that don't affect downstream data flow.\n\nRule of thumb from `resolve_gate_mode()`:\n- Release scope → always BLOCKING\n- Milestone scope → configurable\n- Task scope → TRAILING when `grace_period > 0`\n\n### Parallel Group Pattern\n\nSteps that can run concurrently are wrapped in a list:\n\n```python\nsteps = [\n    single_step_1,\n    [parallel_step_a, parallel_step_b],  # Run concurrently\n    single_step_2,                        # Waits for parallel group\n]\n```\n\nThe generic `execute_pipeline()` handles thread coordination. If using sprint-style custom executor, implement your own parallel dispatch.\n\n### Dependency Rules\n\n- Steps consume outputs of prior steps via `inputs` list\n- A step can only reference outputs from steps that precede it in the graph\n- Parallel steps within a group must not depend on each other\n- Resume logic skips steps whose output already passes their gate\n\n## Model Design Patterns\n\n### Config Model\n\nAlways extend `PipelineConfig`:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    \"\"\"Pipeline-specific configuration.\"\"\"\n    # Required: identify the input\n    source_path: Path\n\n    # Optional: control behavior\n    depth: str = \"standard\"       # quick|standard|deep\n\n    # Computed paths\n    @property\n    def results_dir(self) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / \"results\"\n\n    @property\n    def output_file(self, step_id: str) -> Path:\n        return self.work_dir / f\"{step_id}-output.md\"\n```\n\n### Status Enum\n\nSprint-style pipelines need richer status than generic `StepStatus`:\n\n```python\nclass StepPhaseStatus(Enum):\n    PENDING = \"pending\"\n    RUNNING = \"running\"\n    PASS = \"pass\"\n    PASS_NO_SIGNAL = \"pass_no_signal\"    # Completed but no structured report\n    PASS_NO_REPORT = \"pass_no_report\"    # Output exists but no result file\n    INCOMPLETE = \"incomplete\"             # Budget exhausted\n    HALT = \"halt\"                         # Step recommends stopping\n    TIMEOUT = \"timeout\"                   # Hard timeout exceeded\n    ERROR = \"error\"                       # Process crash\n    SKIPPED = \"skipped\"                   # Skipped by config\n```\n\n### Result Model\n\nExtend `StepResult` with domain telemetry:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyStepResult(StepResult):\n    exit_code: int | None = None\n    started_at: float | None = None\n    finished_at: float | None = None\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    error_bytes: int = 0\n    # Domain-specific fields:\n    artifacts_produced: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)\n    gate_details: dict = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\n### Monitor State\n\nDomain-specific signals extracted from NDJSON output:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyMonitorState:\n    output_bytes: int = 0\n    last_growth_time: float = 0.0\n    events_received: int = 0\n    lines_total: int = 0\n    growth_rate_bps: float = 0.0\n    stall_seconds: float = 0.0\n    # Domain-specific signals:\n    last_step_id: str | None = None\n    current_artifact: str | None = None\n    files_changed: set = field(default_factory=set)\n```\n\n## Gate Design Patterns\n\n### Gate Criteria Tiers\n\n```python\n# Exempt: always passes (for optional/informational steps)\nEXEMPT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[],\n    min_lines=0,\n    enforcement_tier=\"EXEMPT\",\n)\n\n# Light: file exists and non-empty\nLIGHT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[],\n    min_lines=0,\n    enforcement_tier=\"LIGHT\",\n)\n\n# Standard: structural validation\nSTANDARD_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\"title\", \"status\"],\n    min_lines=50,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STANDARD\",\n)\n\n# Strict: structural + semantic validation\nSTRICT_GATE = GateCriteria(\n    required_frontmatter_fields=[\"title\", \"status\", \"convergence_score\"],\n    min_lines=100,\n    enforcement_tier=\"STRICT\",\n    semantic_checks=[\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"no_heading_gaps\",\n            check_fn=_no_heading_gaps,\n            failure_message=\"Heading hierarchy has gaps (e.g. H1→H3 without H2)\",\n        ),\n        SemanticCheck(\n            name=\"refs_resolve\",\n            check_fn=_cross_refs_resolve,\n            failure_message=\"Cross-references do not resolve to valid targets\",\n        ),\n    ],\n)\n```\n\n### Semantic Check Functions\n\nSemantic checks are pure functions that take file content and return `(passed: bool, reason: str)`:\n\n```python\ndef _no_heading_gaps(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify heading hierarchy has no gaps (H1->H3 without H2).\"\"\"\n    # ... implementation ...\n    return (True, \"\") if valid else (False, f\"Heading gap at line {line}\")\n\ndef _has_required_sections(content: str) -> tuple[bool, str]:\n    \"\"\"Verify all required sections are present.\"\"\"\n    required = {\"## Summary\", \"## Findings\", \"## Recommendations\"}\n    present = {line.strip() for line in content.splitlines() if line.startswith(\"## \")}\n    missing = required - present\n    if missing:\n        return (False, f\"Missing sections: {', '.join(missing)}\")\n    return (True, \"\")\n```\n\n### Frontmatter Validation\n\nThe shared `gate_passed()` function handles YAML frontmatter checks. Steps that produce markdown with frontmatter get automatic validation:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Diff Analysis\nstatus: complete\ndiff_points: 12\nconvergence_ready: true\n---\n```\n\n## Prompt Design Patterns\n\n### Prompt Builder Structure\n\nEach step's prompt is a function that takes inputs and returns a complete prompt string:\n\n```python\ndef build_analysis_prompt(source_path: Path, config: MyConfig) -> str:\n    return f\"\"\"Read the source file and produce a structured analysis.\n\nSource: {source_path}\nDepth: {config.depth}\n\n## Required Output Format\n\nWrite your analysis to the output file with this structure:\n\n```yaml\n---\ntitle: Analysis Report\nstatus: complete\nfinding_count: <integer>\n---\n```\n\n## Sections Required\n\n### Summary\nBrief overview of findings.\n\n### Findings\nNumbered list of findings with evidence.\n\n### Recommendations\nActionable next steps.\n\n## Machine-Readable Markers\n\nAt the end of your output, include:\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\n```\nor\n```\nEXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\n```\n\"\"\"\n```\n\n### Key Prompt Rules\n\n1. **Specify output file format** — Tell Claude exactly what frontmatter fields to include\n2. **Require machine-readable markers** — `EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE|HALT` for status determination\n3. **Embed input content when small** — Under ~50KB, embed directly in prompt; otherwise use `--file` args\n4. **Be explicit about sections** — Name every required section; don't leave structure to inference\n5. **Include depth/focus constraints** — If the step has configurable depth, encode it in the prompt\n\n### Input Embedding Pattern\n\n```python\ndef _embed_inputs(prompt: str, inputs: list[Path], config: MyConfig) -> tuple[str, list[str]]:\n    \"\"\"Embed small input files directly into prompt, return file args for large ones.\"\"\"\n    file_args = []\n    for input_path in inputs:\n        full_path = config.work_dir / input_path\n        if full_path.stat().st_size < 50_000:\n            content = full_path.read_text()\n            prompt += f\"\\n\\n---\\n## Input: {input_path}\\n\\n{content}\"\n        else:\n            file_args.append(str(full_path))\n    return prompt, file_args\n```\n\n## Executor Design Patterns\n\n### Sprint-Style Supervisor Loop\n\nThe sprint executor pattern provides supervised execution with monitoring. IMPORTANT: Sprint uses synchronous execution with `threading` for parallelism, NOT `async/await`. Use `time.sleep()` polling loops and `concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor` for batch dispatch.\n\n```python\ndef execute_pipeline(config: MyConfig) -> MyResult:\n    # 1. Pre-flight checks\n    verify_claude_binary()\n\n    # 2. Setup infrastructure\n    signal_handler = SignalHandler()\n    logger = MyLogger(config)\n    tui = MyTUI(config)\n    monitor = OutputMonitor()\n    result = MyResult(config=config)\n    ledger = TurnLedger(initial_budget=config.max_turns)\n\n    # 3. Start TUI\n    tui.start()\n\n    try:\n        for step in config.steps:\n            if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                break\n\n            # 4. Reset monitor for this step\n            monitor.reset(config.output_file(step))\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # 5. Launch Claude subprocess\n            process = ClaudeProcess(config, step)\n            process.start()\n\n            # 6. Supervision loop\n            while process.is_running():\n                if signal_handler.shutdown_requested:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                state = monitor.get_state()\n\n                # Stall detection\n                if state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout:\n                    process.stop()\n                    break\n\n                # TUI update\n                tui.update(step, state)\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # 7. Classify result\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = determine_status(process.exit_code, step, config)\n\n            # 8. Record and decide\n            step_result = build_result(step, status, monitor.state)\n            result.add(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            if status not in (PASS, PASS_NO_SIGNAL):\n                # Collect diagnostics and halt\n                diagnostics = collect_diagnostics(step_result, monitor.state)\n                write_diagnostic_report(diagnostics, config)\n                result.outcome = HALTED\n                break\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        signal_handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n```\n\n### Status Classification\n\nMap every possible exit condition to a deterministic status:\n\n```python\ndef determine_status(exit_code, step, config):\n    # 1. Hard failures\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code != 0:\n        return ERROR\n\n    # 2. Check for structured result file\n    result_path = config.result_file(step)\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return PASS\n        return PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    # 3. Check for output without result\n    output_path = config.output_file(step)\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return INCOMPLETE\n        return PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    # 4. No output at all\n    return ERROR\n```\n\n## Integration Patterns\n\n### main.py Registration\n\n```python\n# In src/superclaude/cli/main.py\nfrom superclaude.cli.my_pipeline import my_pipeline_group\napp.add_command(my_pipeline_group)\n```\n\n### Click Command Group\n\n```python\n@click.group(\"my-pipeline\")\ndef my_pipeline_group():\n    \"\"\"My pipeline description.\"\"\"\n    pass\n\n@my_pipeline_group.command(\"run\")\n@click.argument(\"source\")\n@click.option(\"--depth\", default=\"standard\", type=click.Choice([\"quick\", \"standard\", \"deep\"]))\n@click.option(\"--dry-run\", is_flag=True)\n@click.option(\"--max-turns\", default=25, type=int)\n@click.option(\"--model\", default=None)\n@click.option(\"--debug\", is_flag=True)\ndef run(source, depth, dry_run, max_turns, model, debug):\n    \"\"\"Execute the pipeline.\"\"\"\n    config = load_config(source, depth=depth, dry_run=dry_run, ...)\n    result = execute_pipeline(config)\n    sys.exit(0 if result.success else 1)\n```\n\n## Turn Budget Economics (from unified-audit-gating)\n\nFor pipelines with multiple Claude subprocesses, use `TurnLedger` to manage budget:\n\n```python\nfrom superclaude.cli.sprint.models import TurnLedger\n\n@dataclass\nclass MyConfig(PipelineConfig):\n    max_turns: int = 200\n    min_launch_allocation: int = 10\n    min_remediation_budget: int = 5\n\n# In executor:\nledger = TurnLedger(\n    initial_budget=config.max_turns,\n    minimum_allocation=config.min_launch_allocation,\n    minimum_remediation_budget=config.min_remediation_budget,\n)\n\n# Before launching a step:\nif not ledger.can_launch():\n    result.outcome = HALTED\n    result.halt_reason = \"Budget exhausted\"\n    break\n\n# After step completes, count actual turns used:\nactual_turns = count_turns_from_output(output_path)\nledger.debit(actual_turns)\n\n# If step used fewer turns than allocated, credit back:\nif actual_turns < allocated:\n    ledger.credit(allocated - actual_turns)\n```\n\n## Subprocess Isolation Pattern\n\nFor pipelines spawning child Claude sessions, use the 4-layer isolation model:\n\n```python\ndef setup_isolation(work_dir: Path) -> dict[str, str]:\n    \"\"\"Create isolated environment for child Claude subprocess.\"\"\"\n    env = os.environ.copy()\n\n    # Layer 1: Scoped work directory\n    env[\"CLAUDE_WORK_DIR\"] = str(work_dir)\n\n    # Layer 2: Git ceiling (prevent escaping work_dir)\n    env[\"GIT_CEILING_DIRECTORIES\"] = str(work_dir.parent)\n\n    # Layer 3: Isolated plugin directory\n    plugin_dir = work_dir / \".claude-plugins\"\n    plugin_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_PLUGIN_DIR\"] = str(plugin_dir)\n\n    # Layer 4: Isolated settings\n    settings_dir = work_dir / \".claude-settings\"\n    settings_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    env[\"CLAUDE_SETTINGS_DIR\"] = str(settings_dir)\n\n    return env\n```\n\n## Context Injection Pattern\n\nPrior step results feed into subsequent prompts as compressed context:\n\n```python\ndef build_step_prompt_with_context(step, prior_results: list[StepResult]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Build prompt with prior step context injected.\"\"\"\n    base_prompt = step.prompt\n\n    if not prior_results:\n        return base_prompt\n\n    context_block = \"## Prior Step Context\\n\\n\"\n    for result in prior_results[-3:]:  # Keep recent, compress older\n        context_block += result.to_context_summary(verbose=(result == prior_results[-1]))\n        context_block += \"\\n\\n\"\n\n    return f\"{base_prompt}\\n\\n{context_block}\"\n```\n\n## Resume-First Failure Output Pattern\n\nOn halt, generate actionable resume information:\n\n```python\n@dataclass\nclass MyResult:\n    # ... other fields ...\n\n    def resume_command(self) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Generate CLI command to resume from failure point.\"\"\"\n        if not self.halt_step:\n            return None\n        remaining = [r.step.id for r in self.step_results\n                     if r.status == MyStatus.PENDING]\n        return (\n            f\"superclaude {CLI_NAME} run \"\n            f\"--resume --start {self.halt_step} \"\n            f\"--max-turns {self.suggested_resume_budget}\"\n        )\n\n    @property\n    def suggested_resume_budget(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Estimate turns needed to complete remaining work.\"\"\"\n        remaining_steps = sum(1 for r in self.step_results\n                              if r.status in (MyStatus.PENDING, MyStatus.INCOMPLETE))\n        return remaining_steps * 25  # Default allocation per step\n```\n\n## Pure-Programmatic Step Execution\n\nNot all steps need Claude. Pure-programmatic steps run as direct Python function calls:\n\n```python\ndef execute_step(step, config):\n    \"\"\"Route step to appropriate executor.\"\"\"\n    if step.prompt == \"\":\n        # Reset monitor for this step's output\n            output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n            monitor.reset(output_path)\n            monitor.start()\n\n            # Launch subprocess\n            process = {PREFIX}Process(config, step)\n            logger.write_step_start(step)\n            deadline = time.monotonic() + step.timeout_seconds\n            process.start()\n\n            # Stall watchdog\n                if (config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.stall_seconds > config.stall_timeout\n                        and state.events_received > 0):\n                    if config.stall_action == \"kill\":\n                        process.stop()\n                        break\n\n                try:\n                    tui.update(step, state)\n                except Exception:\n                    pass\n\n                time.sleep(0.5)\n\n            # Classify result\n            exit_code = process.wait()\n            monitor.stop()\n            status = _determine_status(exit_code, step, config)\n\n            step_result = {PREFIX}StepResult(\n                step=step,\n                status=status,\n                exit_code=exit_code,\n                started_at=process.started_at,\n                finished_at=time.time(),\n                output_bytes=monitor.state.output_bytes,\n            )\n            result.step_results.append(step_result)\n            logger.write_step_result(step_result)\n\n            # Finalize\n        if result.outcome == {PREFIX}Outcome.SUCCESS:\n            all_passed = all(\n                r.status in ({PREFIX}Status.PASS, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL, {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT, {PREFIX}Status.SKIPPED)\n                for r in result.step_results\n            )\n            if not all_passed:\n                result.outcome = {PREFIX}Outcome.ERROR\n\n        result.finished_at = time.time()\n        logger.write_summary(result)\n\n    finally:\n        tui.stop()\n        monitor.stop()\n        handler.restore()\n\n    return result\n\n\n{BUILD_STEPS_FUNCTION}\n\n\ndef _determine_status(\n    exit_code: int | None,\n    step,\n    config: {PREFIX}Config,\n) -> {PREFIX}Status:\n    \"\"\"Classify step outcome from exit code and output artifacts.\"\"\"\n    if exit_code == 124:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.TIMEOUT\n    if exit_code and exit_code != 0:\n        return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n\n    result_path = config.work_dir / f\"{step.id}-result.md\"\n    output_path = config.work_dir / step.output_file\n\n    if result_path.exists():\n        content = result_path.read_text()\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: HALT\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        if \"EXIT_RECOMMENDATION: CONTINUE\" in content:\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: PASS\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.PASS\n        if \"status: FAIL\" in content.lower():\n            return {PREFIX}Status.HALT\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_SIGNAL\n\n    if output_path.exists():\n        if detect_error_max_turns(output_path):\n            return {PREFIX}Status.INCOMPLETE\n        return {PREFIX}Status.PASS_NO_REPORT\n\n    return {PREFIX}Status.ERROR\n```\n\n## Template: `monitor.py`\n\nFollow the sprint monitor pattern exactly — incremental NDJSON tail with signal extraction. On any validation failure, the command emits an error and exits without invoking the skill. Strip `sc-` prefix if present\n2. Strip `-protocol` suffix if present\n3. Convert to kebab-case for CLI, snake_case for Python modules\n\n## Input Validation\n\nBefore invoking the skill, validate all inputs. On any validation failure, emit an error and exit without invoking the skill.\n\n**Error format:**\n```\nerror_code: <ERROR_CODE>\nmessage: <human-readable description with corrective action>\n```\n\n**Validation checks:**\n\n1. **Workflow argument present**: `--workflow` must be provided.\n   - Error: `error_code: MISSING_WORKFLOW` / `message: \"--workflow is required. Provide a skill directory path or sc-* name.\"`\n\n2. **Workflow path resolves**: The workflow path resolves to a directory containing `SKILL.md`.\n   - Error: `error_code: INVALID_PATH` / `message: \"Path '<path>' does not exist or does not contain a SKILL.md file.\"`\n\n3. **Workflow path unambiguous**: Only one candidate directory matches the workflow name.\n   - Error: `error_code: AMBIGUOUS_PATH` / `message: \"Multiple candidates found for '<name>': <list>. Use a full path to disambiguate.\"`\n\n4. **Output directory writable**: If `--output` is provided, its parent directory exists and is writable.\n   - Error: `error_code: OUTPUT_NOT_WRITABLE` / `message: \"Output directory parent '<parent>' does not exist or is not writable.\"`\n\n5. **No name collision**: The derived or provided `--name` does not collide with an existing non-portified CLI module.\n   - Error: `error_code: NAME_COLLISION` / `message: \"CLI module '<name>' already exists at '<path>' and was not generated by portification. Use --name to specify an alternative.\"`\n\n6. **Name derivation succeeds**: If `--name` is not provided, derivation from the workflow name produces a valid identifier.\n   - Error: `error_code: DERIVATION_FAILED` / `message: \"Could not derive CLI name from workflow '<name>'. Use --name to specify explicitly.\"`\n\n## Activation\n\n**Classification**: STRICT -- multi-file code generation operation with API conformance requirements.\n\n**MANDATORY**: Before executing any protocol steps, invoke:\n> Skill sc:cli-portify-protocol\n\nPass the following context:\n- Workflow path: resolved path to the skill directory\n- CLI name: resolved name (derived or from --name)\n- Output directory: resolved output path\n- Dry run: boolean flag value\n- Skip integration: boolean flag value\n\nDo NOT attempt to execute portification using only this command file.\nThe full portification protocol is in the protocol skill.\n\n## Examples\n\n```bash\n# Basic: portify a skill\n/sc:cli-portify --workflow src/superclaude/skills/sc-cleanup-audit/\n\n# With explicit name\n/sc:cli-portify --workflow sc-cleanup-audit --name cleanup-audit\n\n# Dry run (analysis only, no code generation)\n/sc:cli-portify --workflow sc-adversarial --dry-run\n\n# Skip main.py integration\n/sc:cli-portify --workflow sc-roadmap --skip-integration\n\n# Full invocation\n/sc:cli-portify --workflow src/superclaude/skills/sc-tasklist-protocol/ --name tasklist --output src/superclaude/cli/tasklist/\n```\n\n## Boundaries\n\n**Will:**\n- Parse and validate input arguments\n- Derive CLI name from workflow name\n- Resolve workflow path to a skill directory\n- Invoke the
